      Konāmeso dhammo sutasoma 
 Kā ca nāma pabbajjā    
 Yaṃ no ambha jiṇṇo 
 Anapekko pabbajasi deva  
  
                    
      Puttāpi tuyhaṃ bahavo 
 Daharā appattayobbanā mañaju te    taṃ apassantā 
 Maññe dukkhaṃ nigacchanti  
  
   Parissaje   machasaṃ   Pabbajjāyaṃ   machasaṃ   Tepi   machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Puttehi ca me etehi  
 Daharehi appatatayobbatehi  
 Mañajuhi sabbehipi tumebhahi 
 Cirampi ṭhatvā vinābhāvo  
  
      Chinnaṃ nu tuyhaṃ hadayaṃ 
 Ādu    karuṇā ca natthi ambhesu  
 Yaṃ no vikkandattiyo 
 Anapekkho pabbajasi deva  
  
                    
      Na ca mayahaṃ chinnaṃ hadayaṃ 
 Atthi karuṇāpi myahaṃ tumbhesu  
 Saggañca patthayāno 
 Tenāhaṃ pabbajissāmi  
  
      Dulladdhaṃ me āsi sutaso 
 Yassa te ahaṃ bhariyā  
 Yaṃ me vilapantiyā 
 Anapekkho pabbajasi deva  
      Dulladdhaṃ me āsi sutaso 
 Yassa te ahaṃ bhariyā  
 Yaṃ me kucchipaṭisandhiṃ 
 Anapekkho pabbajasi deva  
  
      Paripakko me gabbho 
 Kucchigato yāva naṃ vijāyāmi  
 Māhaṃ eko vidhavā 
 Pacchā dukkhāni addakkhiṃ    
                    
      Paripakko te    gabbho 
 Kucchigato iṅgha tvaṃ    vijāyassu  
 Puttaṃ anomavaṇṇaṃ 
 Taṃ hitvā pabbajissāmi  
  
      Mā tvaṃ cande rudi 
 Mā sovi vanatimiramattakkhi  
 Āroha varapāsādaṃ 
 Anapekkho ahaṃ gamissāmi  
      Ko taṃ amma kopesi 
 Kiṃ rodasi pekkhasi ca maṃ baḷhaṃ  
 Kaṃ    avajjhaṃ ghātemi 
 Ñātinaṃ udikkhamānānaṃ  
  
   Ādute   machasaṃ   Adakkhiṃ   machasaṃ   Ca te   machasaṃ   Naṃ vi   machasaṃ   
 Taṃ avajjhaṃ   machasaṃ  
                    
      Nahi so sakkā hantuṃ  
 Vijitāvi yo maṃ tāta kopesi  
 Pitā te maṃ tāta avaca 
 Anapekkho ahaṃ gamissāmi  
  
      Yāhaṃ pubbe niyyāmi 
 Uyyānaṃ    kuñajare    ca yodhemi  
 Sutasome    pababajite 
 Kathannudāni karissāmi  
  
      Mātu ca me rudantyā    
 Jeṭṭhassa ca bhātuno akāmassa  
 Hatthepi te gahessaṃ    
 Na hi gacchasi no akāmānaṃ  
  
                    
      Uṭṭhehi tvaṃ dhāni 
 Imaṃ kumāraṃ    ramehi aññattha  
 Mā me paripatthamakā    
 Saggaṃ mama patthayānassa  
  
      Yannunimaṃ dadeyyaṃ    sabhaṅkaraṃ 
 Ko nu me iminā attho  
 Sutasome pabbajite 
 Kinnu me taṃ karissāmi  
  
      Koso ca tuyhaṃ vipulo 
 Koṭṭhāgārañca tuyhaṃ paripuraṃ  
 Paṭhavi    ca tuyhaṃ vijitā      
 Ramassu mā pabbajassu deva  
      Koso ca tuyhaṃ vipulo 
 Koṭṭhāgārañca mayhaṃ paripuraṃ  
 Paṭhavi ca mayhaṃ vijitā  
 Taṃ hitvā pabbajissāmi  
                    
      Mayhampi dhanaṃ pahutaṃ 
 Saṅkhyātuṃ nopi deva sakkomi  
 Taṃ deva te dadāmi sabbampi 
 Ramassu mā pabbaja deva  
  
   Sohaṃ pubbe rathena yāmi uyyānaṃ   machasaṃ   Matta kuñajareva yodemi   machasaṃ 
 syā   Sutasoma   machasaṃ   Rudāntarā   machasaṃ 
   Gamissaṃ   vi machasaṃ gahissaṃ   syā   Kumārī   machasaṃ kumāraṃ kumāri   vi 
   Paribandhamakāsi   machasaṃ   Dadeyya   vi machasaṃ   Pathavi   machasaṃ 
    Vijitāvi  
  
                     
      Jānāmi te dhanaṃ pahutaṃ 
 Kulavaḍḍhana pujito tayā casmi  
 Saggañca patthayāno 
 Tenāhaṃ pabbajissāmi  
  
      Ukkaṇṭhitosmi bāḷhaṃ 
 Arati maṃ somadanta āvisati  
 Bahukā hi antarāyā 
 Ajjevāhaṃ pabbajissāmi  
  
      Idampi tuyhaṃ rucitaṃ sutasoma 
 Ajjevadāni tvaṃ pabbaja  
 Ahampi pabbajissāmi 
 Na ussahe tayā vinā ahaṃ ṭhātuṃ  
  
                    
      Na hi sakkā pabbajituṃ  
 Nagare na ha paccati janapade ca  
 Sutasome pabbajite 
 Kathannudāni karissāma  
  
      Upaniyatidaṃ maññe 
 Parittaṃ udakaṃva caṅgavārambhi  
 Evaṃ suparittake jivite 
 Na ca pamajjituṃ kālo  
      Upaniyatidaṃ maññe 
 Parittaṃ udakaṃva caṅgavārambhi  
 Evaṃ suparittake jivite 
 Atha bālā pamajjanti  
  
      Te vaḍḍhayanti nirayaṃ 
 Tiracchānayoniñca pettivisayañca  
 Taṇhābandhanabaddhā 
 Vaḍḍhenti asurakāyaṃ  
  
                    
      Ūhaññate rajaggaṃ 
 Avidūre pupphakambhi pāsāde  
 Maññe no kesā chinnā 
 Yasassino dhammarājassa  
  
      Ayamassa pāsādo 
 Sovaṇṇapupphamāpāyavitikiṇṇo  
 Yabhimanuvicarī rājā 
 Parikiṇṇo itthāgārehi  
  
                    
      Ayamassa pāsādo 
 Sovaṇṇapupphamāpāyavitikiṇṇo  
 Yabhimanuvicarī rājā 
 Parikiṇṇo ñātisaṅghena  
  
      Idhamassa kūṭāgāraṃ 
 Sovaṇṇapupphamāpāyavitikiṇṇo  
 Yabhimanuvicarī rājā 
 Parikiṇṇo itthāgārehi  
  
      Idhamassa kūṭāgāraṃ 
 Sovaṇṇapupphamāpāyavitikiṇṇo  
 Yabhimanuvicarī rājā 
 Parikiṇṇo ñātisaṅghena  
  
      Ayamassa asokavanikā  
 Supupphitā sabbakālikā rammā  
 Yabhimanuvicarī rājā 
 Parikiṇṇo itthāgārehi  
  
      Ayamassa asokavanikā  
 Supupphitā sabbakālikā rammā  
 Yabhimanuvicarī rājā 
 Parikiṇṇo ñātisaṅghena  
  
                    
      Idhamassa uyyānaṃ  
 Supupphitā sabbakālikā rammā  
 Yabhimanuvicarī rājā 
 Parikiṇṇo itthāgārehi  
  
      Idamassa uyyānaṃ 
 Supupphitā sabbakālikā rammā  
 Yabhimanuvicarī rājā 
 Parikiṇṇo ñātisaṅghena  
  
      Idamassa kaṇikāravanaṃ  
 Supupphitā sabbakālikā rammā  
 Yabhimanuvicarī rājā 
 Parikiṇṇo itthāgārehi  
  
      Idamassa kaṇikāravanaṃ  
 Supupphitā sabbakālikā rammā  
 Yabhimanuvicarī rājā 
 Parikiṇṇo ñātisaṅghena 
  
      Idamassa pāṭaḷivanaṃ  
 Supupphitā sabbakālikā rammā  
 Yabhimanuvicarī rājā 
 Parikiṇṇo itthāgārehi  
  
                    
      Idamassa pāṭaḷivanaṃ  
 Supupphitā sabbakālikā rammā  
 Yabhimanuvicarī rājā 
 Parikiṇṇo ñātisaṅghena  
  
      Idamassa ambavanaṃ  
 Supupphitā sabbakālikā rammā  
 Yabhimanuvicarī rājā 
 Parikiṇṇo itthāgārehi  
  
      Idamassa ambavanaṃ  
 Supupphitā sabbakālikā rammā  
 Yabhimanuvicarī rājā 
 Parikiṇṇo ñātisaṅghena  
  
                    
      Ayamassa pokkharaṇi 
 Sañachantā aṇḍajehi vitikiṇṇā yabhimanuvicarī rājā 
 Parikiṇṇo itthāgārehi  
  
      Ayamassa pokkharaṇi 
 Sañachantā aṇḍajehi vitikiṇṇā yabhimanuvicarī rājā 
 Parikiṇṇo ñātisaṅghena  
  
      Rājā kho pabbajito 
 Sutasomo rajjaṃ imaṃ pahatvāna  
 Kāsāyavatthasano 
 Nāgova ekakova carati  
  
                    
      Māssu pubbe ratikiḷitāni 
 Hasitāni anussarittha  
 Mā vo kāmā haniṃsu 
 Rammaṃ hi sudassanaṃ nāma nagaraṃ  
  
      Mentaṃ cittañca hāvetha 
 Appamāṇaṃ divā ca ratto ca  
 Atha gañachittha devapuraṃ 
 Āvāsaṃ puññakamminanti  
 Cullasutasomajātakaṃ  
  
 Cattāḷisanipāto niṭṭhito  
 Tassuddānaṃ  
 Suvapaṇḍitajambukakuṇḍalino 
 Sarabhaṅgamalambusajātakañca  
 Pavaruttamasaṅkhasirivhayako 
 Sutasoma arindama rājavaroti  
  
                    
  
   Nalinikājātakaṃ  
                    
      Uḍḍhayhate    janapado raṭṭhañcāpi vinassati  
 Ehi nalinike    gaccha taṃ me brāhmaṇamānaya  
  
      Nāhaṃ dukkhakkhamā rāja nāhaṃ addhānakovidā  
 Kathaṃ ahaṃ gamissāmi vanaṃ kuñajarasevitaṃ  
  
      Phītaṃ janadaṃ gantvā hatthinā ca rathena ca  
 Dārusaṅghāṭayānena evaṃ gaccha nalinike    
  
                    
      Katthi assā rathā patti    gacchevādāya khantiye  
 Taveva vaṇṇarūpena vasaṃ taṃ ānayissasi  
  
      Kadalidhajapaññāṇo ābhujiparivārito  
 Eso padissati rammo isisiṅgassa assamo  
  
      Eso aggissa saṅkhāto eso dhumo padissati  
 Maññe no agagiṃ hāpeti isisiṅgo mahiddhiko  
  
      Tañca disvāna āyantiṃ āmuttamaṇikuṇḍalaṃ    
 Isisiṅgo pāvisi bhito assamaṃ paṇṇachādanaṃ  
  
      Assamassa ca sā dvāre bheṇḍukenassa kīḷati  
 Vidaṃsayanti aṅgāni guyhaṃ pakāsitāni ca  
      Tañe disvāna kīḷantiṃ    paṇṇasālagato jaṭī  
 Assamā nikkhamitvāna idaṃ vacanamabravi  
  
      Ambho ko nāma so rukkho yassa tevaṃgataṃ phalaṃ  
 Durepi khittaṃ pacceti na taṃ ohāya gacchati  
  
      Assamassa mamaṃ    buhme samipe gandhamādane  
 Pabbateta tādisā rukkhā yasasa tevaṅgataṃ phalaṃ 
 Durepi khittaṃ pacceti na maṃ ohāya gacchati    
  
   Udayahate   machasaṃ   Niḷinike   machasaṃ   Hatthi assa rathe patatiṃ   machasaṃ   
 Kuṇḍaliṃ   machasaṃ   Kiḷanti   machasaṃ   Mama   machasaṃ 
   Gacchatha   machasaṃ syā 
  
                    
    page      
      Etu bhavaṃ assamimaṃ adetu 
 Pajjañca bhakkhañca paṭiccha dammi  
 Idamāsanaṃ atra bhavaṃ nisidatu 
 Ito bhavaṃ mulaphalāni khādatu    
  
      Kinte idaṃ ūrunamantarasamiṃ 
 Supicchitaṃ kaṇharivappakāsati  
 Akkhāhi me pucachito etamatthaṃ 
 Akosenu te uttamaṅgaṃ paviṭṭhaṃ  
  
                    
      Ahaṃ vane mulaphalesanaṃ caraṃ 
 Āsādayiṃ    acchaṃ sughorarūpaṃ  
 So maṃ patitvā sahasajjhapanto    
 Panujja maṃ abbahi    uttamaṅgaṃ  
  
      Svāyaṃ vaṇo khajjati kaṇḍuvāyati 
 Sabbañca kālaṃ na labhāmi sātaṃ  
 Paho bhavaṃ kaṇḍumimaṃ vinetuṃ 
 Kurutaṃ bhavaṃ yācito brāhmaṇattha  
  
      Gambhirarūpo te vaṇo salohito 
 Apūtiko pakkagandho mahā ca  
 Karomi te kiñci kasāyayogaṃ 
 Yathā bhavaṃ paramasukhī bhaveyya  
  
      Na mantayogā na kasāvayogā 
 Na osadhā brahmacāri kamanti  
 Yaṃ te mudu tena vinehi kaṇḍu 
 Yathā ahaṃ paramasukhī bhaveyyaṃ  
  
                    
      Ito nu bhoto katamena assamo 
 Kacci bhavaṃ abhiramasi araññe  
 Kaccinu te mulaphalaṃ pahutaṃ    
 Kacci bhavantaṃ na vihiṃsanti vāḷā  
      Ito ujuṃ utatarāyaṃ disāyaṃ 
 Khemā nadi himavantā pahāti    
 Tassā tīre assamo mayha rammo 
 Aho bhavaṃ assamaṃ mayha passe  
  
   Bhuñjatuṃ   vi machasaṃ   Asādayi   machasaṃ   Sahasā   machasaṃ 
   Abbhuhi   machasaṃ   Bahutaṃ   machasaṃ   Khemānadi himavatāpahavi   machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Ambā ca sālā tilakā ca jambuyo 
 Uddālakā pāṭaliyo ca phullā  
 Samantato kimpurisābhigitaṃ 
 Aho bhavaṃ assamaṃ mayaha    passe  
  
                    
      Tālā ca mulā ca phalā ca mettha 
 Vaṇṇena gandhena upetarūpā  
 Taṃ bhūmibhāgehi upetarūpaṃ 
 Aho bhavaṃ assamaṃ mayha passe  
  
      Phalā ca mulā ca pahuta    mettha 
 Vaṇṇena gandhena rasenupetā  
 Āyanti ca luddakā naṃ padesaṃ 
 Mā me tato mulaphalaṃ abhāsuṃ    
  
      Pitā mamaṃ pulaphalesanaṃ gato 
 Idāni āgacchati sāyakāle    
 Ubhova gacchāmase asasamaṃ taṃ 
 Yāva pitā mulaphalate etu  
  
                    
      Aññe bahu isayo sādhurūpā 
 Rājisayo anumagge vasanti  
 Teyeva pucchesi mamassamaṃ taṃ 
 Te taṃ nayissanti mamaṃ sakāse  
  
      Na te kaṭṭhāni bhintāni na te udakamābhataṃ  
 Aggipi te na bhāsito    kinnu mandova jhāyasi  
  
      Hinnāni kaṭṭhāni huto ca aggi 
 Tapanipi    te samitā brahmacāri  
 Piṭhañca mayhaṃ udakañca hoti 
 Ramasi tvaṃ brahmabhūto puratthā  
  
      Abhintakaṭṭhosi anābhatodako 
 Abhāsitaggisi asiddhabhojano  
 Na me tuvaṃ ālapasi mamajja 
 Naṭṭhannu kiṃ cetasikañca dukkhaṃ  
  
   Mayhaṃ   vi machasaṃ   Bahutā   machasaṃ   Ahesuṃ   machasaṃ 
   Sayānukāhe   machasaṃ   Kahāpito   machasaṃ   Tapanipito   machasaṃ 
  
                    
                    
      Idhāgamā jaṭilo brahmacāri 
 Sudassaneyyo sutanu vineti  
 Nevātidigo napanātirasso 
 Sukaṇhakaṇhacchadanehi bhoto  
  
      Amassujāno apurāṇavaṇṇi 
 Ādhārarūpañca panassa kaṇṭhe  
 Dvepassa    gaṇḍā ure sujātā 
 Suvaṇṇapiṇḍupanibhā    pabhassarā  
  
      Mukhañca tassa bhusa    dasasaneyyaṃ 
 Kaṇṇesu lambanti ca kuñcitaggā  
 Te jotare carato māṇavassa 
 Suttañca yaṃ saṃyamanaṃ jaṭānaṃ  
      Aññā ca tassa saññamani catasso 
 Nīlā pitā lohitikā ca setā  
 Tā saṃsare carato māṇavassa 
 Cirīṭisaṅghāriva pāvusambhi    
  
                    
      Na mekhalaṃ    muñajamayaṃ dhareti 
 Na santace    no pana babbajassa    
 Tā jotare jaghanantare    visanatā 
 Sateritā vijjurivantalikkhe  
  
      Akhilakāni ca avaṇṭakāni 
 Heṭṭhā nābhyā    kaṭisamohitāni  
 Aghaṭṭitā niccakiliṃ karonti 
 Haṃ tāta kiṃ rukkhaphalāni tāti  
  
      Jaṭā ca tassa bhusadassaneyyā 
 Parosataṃ vellitaggā sugandhā  
 Dvedhāsiro sādhuvibhattarūpo 
 Aho nukho mayha tathā jaṭāssu  
  
      Yadā ca so pakirati tā jaṭāyo 
 Vaṇṇena gandhena upetarūpā  
 Niluppalaṃ vātasameritaṃva tatheva saṃvāti vanasasamo ayaṃ  
  
   Veyamāgandhā   machasaṃ veyamāgaṇḍā   syā   Na mikhalaṃ   machasaṃ 
   Suvaṇṇatiṇḍuka nibhā   machasaṃ   Nasantare no   machasaṃ 
   Bhūsaṃ   machasaṃ   Pabbajasasa   si 
   Tāviṃsare   machasaṃ   Jaṅghanantare   machasaṃ   Nabhyā   machasaṃ  
  
                    
      Paṅko ca tassa bhusadassaneyyo 
 Netādiso yādiso mayhakāyo  
 So vāyati erito māḷutena 
 Vanaṃ yathā aggagimbhe suphullaṃ  
  
      Nihanti so rukkhaphalaṃ paṭhabyā 
 Sucittarūpaṃ ruciraṃ dassaneyyaṃ  
 Khittañca tassa punareti hatthaṃ 
 Haṃ tāta kiṃ rukkhaphalaṃ nu kho taṃ  
  
      Dantā ca tassa bhusadassaneyyā 
 Suddhā samā saṅkhavarūpapantā  
 Mano pasādenti vivariyamānā 
 Naha nūna so sākamakhādi tehi  
  
                    
      Akakkasaṃ agaḷitaṃ    muhuṃ muduṃ 
 Ujuṃ anuddhataṃ avapalamassa bhāsitaṃ  
 Rudaṃ manuññaṃ karavitasussaraṃ 
 Hadayaṅgamaṃ rañajayateva me mano 
  
      Bindussaro nātivissaṭṭhavākyo 
 Na nūna sajjhāyamatippayutto  
 Icchāmi kho    taṃ punareva    daṭṭhuṃ 
 Mittaṃ hi me māṇavāhu puratthā  
  
      Susandhi sabbattha vimaṭṭhimaṃ vaṇaṃ 
 Puthu sujātaṃ kharapattasannibhaṃ  
 Teneva maṃ uttariyāna māṇavo 
 Vivariya ūruṃ jaghatena piḷayi  
  
      Tapanti ābhanti virocare ca 
 Sateratā vijjurivantalikkhe  
 Bāhā mudu añajanalomasādisā 
 Vicitravaṭṭaṅgulikāssa sobhare  
  
      Akakkasaṅgo na ca dighalomo 
 Nakhassa dīghā api lohitaggā  
 Muduhi bāhihi paḷissajanto 
 Kalyāṇarūpo ramayaṃ upaṭṭhahi  
  
   Aggalitaṃ   machasaṃ   Bho   machasaṃ   Putadeva   machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Dumassa tulupanibhā pabhassarā 
 Suvaṇṇakambutalavaṭṭasucchavi  
 Hatthā mudu tehi maṃ samphusitvā 
 Ito gato te maṃ dahanti tāta  
  
      Naha nūna so khārividhaṃ ahāsi 
 Na nūna kaṭṭhāhi sayaṃ abhañaji  
 Na nūna so hanti dume kuṭhāriyā 
 Na pissa hatthesu khilāni atthi  
  
                    
      Accho ca kho tassa vaṇaṃ akhāsi 
 So maṃ bravi sukhitaṃ maṃ karohi  
 Tāhaṃ kariṃ tena mamāsi sobyaṃ 
 So maṃ bravi sukhitosamiti brahema  
  
      Ayañca te māluvapaṇṇasatthatā 
 Vikiṇṇarūpāva mayā ca tena ca  
 Kilanantarūpā udake ramitvā 
 Punappunaṃ paṇṇakuṭiṃ vajāma  
  
      Na majja mantā paṭibhanti tāta 
 Na aggihuttaṃ napi yaññatantraṃ  
 Na cāpi te mulaphalāni bhuñeja 
 Yāva na passāmi taṃ brahmacāriṃ  
  
      Addhā pajānāsi tuvampi tāta 
 Yassaṃ disāyaṃ vasate brahmacāri  
 Taṃ maṃ disā pāpaya tāta khippaṃ 
 Mā te ahaṃ amariṃ assamambhi  
  
      Vicitrapupphaṃ hi vanaṃ sutaṃ mayā 
 Dijābhighuṭṭhaṃ dijasaṅghasevitaṃ  
 Taṃ maṃ vanaṃ pāpaya tāta khippaṃ 
 Purā te pāṇaṃ vijahāmi assame  
  
                    
      Imasmāhaṃ jotirase vanambhi 
 Gandhabbadevaccharasaṅghasevite  
 Isinamāvāse sanantanamabhi 
 Netādisaṃ aratiṃ pāpuṇetha  
  
                    
      Bhavanti mittāni atho na honti 
 Ñātisu mittesu karonti pemaṃ  
 Ayañca jammo kissa vā niviṭṭho 
 Yo neva jānātikutombhi āgato  
  
      Saṃvāsena hi mittāni sandhiyanti punappunaṃ  
 Seca va mitto aghaṅgattu asaṃvāsena jirati  
  
      Sace tuvaṃ dakkhasi buhmacāriṃ 
 Sace tuvaṃ sallapi    brahmacārinā  
 Sampannasasasaṃ va mahodakena 
 Tapoguṇaṃ khippamimaṃ pahassasi    
  
      Punapi ce dakkhasi brahmacāriṃ 
 Punapi ce sallape brahmacārinā  
 Sampannasassaṃ va mahodakena 
 Usmāgataṃ khippamimaṃ pabhassasi    
  
      Bhūtāni hetāni caranti tāta 
 Virūparūpena manussaloke  
 Nana tāti sevetha nāro sapañño 
 Āsajja naṃ nassati brahmacāriti  
 Nalinikājātakaṃ  
  
   Ummādanatījātakaṃ                    
      Nivesanaṃ kassa nudaṃ sutanda 
 Pākārena paṇḍumayena guttaṃ kā disasti agagisikhāva dure 
 Vehāsayaṃ    pabbataggeva acci  
  
      Dhītānayaṃ kassa sunandaṃ hoti 
 Suṇisānayaṃ kassa athopi bhariyā  
 Akkhāhi me khipapamidheva puṭṭho 
 Avāvaṭā yadi vā atthi bhattā 
  
                    
      Ahaṃ hi jānāmi janinda etaṃ 
 Matyā ca petyā ca athopi assā  
 Taveva so puriso bhumipāla 
 Rattindivaṃ appamato tavatthe  
  
   Pallape   vi machasaṃ   Pahissasi   machasaṃ   Pahissati   machasaṃ 
   Vehāyasaṃ   machasaṃ syā  
  
                    
      Iddho ca phito ca suvaḍḍhi    to ca 
 Amacco ca te aññataro janinda  
 Tassosā    bhariyā abhipārakassa 
 Ummādanti    nāmadheyyena rāja  
  
      Ambho ambho nāmamidaṃ imissā 
 Matyā ca petyā ca kataṃ susādhu  
 Tathā hi    mayhaṃ avalokayanti 
 Ummattakaṃ ummadanti akāsi  
  
                    
      Sā puṇṇamāse vigamandalocanā 
 Upāvisi puṇḍarikattacaṅgī  
 Dve puṇṇamāyo tadahu amaññaṃ 
 Disvāna pārāvatarattavāsiniṃ  
  
      Aḷārapambhehi subhehi vagguhi 
 Palobhayanti maṃ yadā udikkhati  
 Vijambhamānā harateva me mano 
 Jātā vane nimpurisiva pabbate  
  
      Tadā hi buhati sāmā āmuttamaṇikuṇḍalā  
 Ekaccavasanā nāri migi bhantāvudikkhati  
  
      Kadāssu maṃ tambanakhā sulomā 
 Bāhā mudu candanasāralittā  
 Vaṭṭaṅguli santatadhirakuttiyā 
 Nāri upaññisasti sisato subhā  
  
      Kadāssu maṃ kañcanajāluracchadā 
 Dhitā tiriṭissa vilākamajjhā  
 Muhuhi bāhāhi paḷissajisasti 
 Brahāvane jātadumaṃva māluvā  
  
      Kadāssu lākhārasarattasucchavi 
 Khindutthani puṇḍarikattacaṅgi  
 Mukhaṃ mukhena upanāmayissati 
 Soṇḍo soṇḍassa surāya thālaṃ  
  
   Suvaddhī  machasaṃ   Tasseva   machasaṃ syā   Ummādayantitahi   machasaṃ 
 Ummādanatīti syā   Tadāhi   machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Yadāddaṃ taṃ tiṭṭhantiṃ sabbagattaṃ manoramaṃ  
 Tato sakassa cittassa nāvabodhāmi kañcinaṃ  
  
      Ummādantimahaṃ diṭṭho āmuttamaṇikuṇḍalaṃ  
 Na supāmi divārattiṃ sahassaṃva parājito  
  
                    
      Sakko ca me vararaṃ dajjā so ca labbhetha me varo  
 Ekarattaṃ dirattaṃ vā bhaveyyaṃ abhipārako 
 Ummādantyā ramitvāna sivirājā tato siyaṃ  
  
                    
      Bhūtāni me bhūtapati namassato 
 Āgamma yakkho idamevamabravi    
 Rañño mano ummadantyā niviṭṭho 
 Dadāmi te taṃ paricārayassu  
      Puññā vidhaṃse    amaro na camahi 
 Jano ca me pāpamidanti jaññā  
 Bhuso ca tyassa manaso vighāto 
 Datvā piyaṃ ummadantiṃ adiṭṭhā  
  
      Janinda nāññatu tayā mayā vā 
 Sabbāpi kammassa katassa jaññā  
 Yante mayā ummadanti padintā 
 Bhusehi rājā vanathaṃ sajāhi  
  
                    
      Yo pāpakaṃ kammakaraṃ manusso 
 So maññati māyidaṃ maññiṃsu aññe  
 Passanti bhūtāni karontametaṃ 
 Yuttā va ye honti narā paṭhabyā  
  
      Añño nu te koci naro paṭhabyā 
 Saddaheyya    lokasmiṃ na me piyāti  
 Bhuso ca tyassa manaso vighāto 
 Datvā piyaṃ ummadantiṃ adiṭṭhā  
  
      Addhā piyā mayha janinda esā 
 Na sā mama appiyā bhūmipāla  
 Gaccheva tvaṃ ummadantiṃ bhadante 
 Sīhova selassa guhaṃ upehi  
   Idametadabravi   vi machasaṃ syā   Puñña vadhaṃse   machasaṃ puññā ca dhaṃse   syā 
   Saddheyya   vi machasaṃ  
  
                    
  
      Na piḷitā attadukkhena dhīrā 
 Sukhapphalaṃ kammaṃ paricchajanti  
 Sammohitāvāpi sukhena mattā 
 Na pāpakammañca samācaranti  
  
      Tuvañhi mātā ca pitā ca mayhaṃ 
 Bhattā pati posako devatā ca  
 Dāso ahaṃ tuyha saputtadāro 
 Yathā sukhaṃ sibba karohi kāmaṃ  
  
      Yo issarombhīti kāroti pāpaṃ  
 Katvā ca so nuttapate    paresaṃ  
 Na tena so jīvati dīghamāyuṃ 
 Devāpi pāpena samekkhare naṃ  
  
      Aññatakaṃ sāmikehi padintaṃ 
 Dhamme ṭhitā ye paṭicchanti dānaṃ  
 Paṭicchakā dāyakā cāpi tattha 
 Sukhappaphalaññeva karonati kammaṃ  
  
                    
      Añño nu te koci naro paṭhabyā 
 Saddaheyya    lokasmiṃ na me piyāti  
 Bhuso ca tyassa manaso vighāto 
 Datvā piyaṃ ummadantiṃ adiṭṭhā    
  
      Addhā piyā mayha janinda esā 
 Na sā mama    appiyā bhūmipāla  
 Yante mayā ummadanti padinnā 
 Bhusehi rājā vanathaṃ sajāhi  
  
      Yo attadukkhena parasasa dukkhaṃ 
 Sukhena vā attasukhaṃ dahāti  
 Yathevidaṃ mayha tathā paresaṃ 
 Yo evaṃ jānāti savedi dhammaṃ  
  
      Añño nu te koci nāro paṭhabyā 
 Saddaheyya lokasmiṃ na me piyāti  
 Bhuso ca tyassa manaso vighāto 
 Datvā piyaṃ ummadantiṃ adiṭṭhā  
  
   Nuttasate   machasaṃ   Saddheyya   vi machasaṃ   Diṭṭhā   machasaṃ 
   Mamaṃ   vi machasaṃ  
  
                    
      Janinda jānāsi piyā mamesā 
 Na sā mamaṃ appiyā bhūmipāla  
 Piyena te dammi piyaṃ janinda 
 Piyadāyino deva piyaṃ labhanti  
  
      So nunāhaṃ vadhissāmi attānaṃ kāmahetukaṃ  
 Tahi dhammaṃ adhammena ahaṃ vidhitumusasahe  
  
      Sace tuvaṃ mayha satiṃ janinda 
 Na kāmayāsi raviraseṭṭha  
 Cajāmi naṃ sabbajanassa sibba 
 Mayā pamutataṃ tato avhayesi naṃ  
  
      Adusiyaṃ ce abhipāraka tvaṃ 
 Cajāsi katte ahitāya tyassa vahā    ca te upavādopi assa 
 Na cāpi tyassa nagarambhī pakkho  
  
      Ahaṃ sabhissaṃ upavādametaṃ 
 Nindaṃ pasaṃsaṃ garahañca sabbaṃ  
 Mametamāgacchatu bhūmipāla 
 Yathā sukhaṃ sibba    karohi kāmaṃ  
  
                    
      Yo neva nindaṃ na punappasaṃsaṃ    
 Ādiyati garahaṃ nopi pujaṃ  
 Siri ca lakkhī ca apeti tamhā 
 Āpo suvuṭṭhiva yathā thalambhā  
  
      Yaṃ kiñci dukkhaṃ ca sukhañca etto 
 Dhammātisārañca manovighātaṃ  
 Urasā ahaṃ paṭicchissāmi sabbaṃ 
 Paṭhavi yathā thāvarānaṃ tasānaṃ  
  
      Dhammātisārañca manovighātaṃ 
 Dukkhaṃ ca nicchāmi ahaṃ paresaṃ  
 Ekopimaṃ tārayissāmi ahaṃ bhāraṃ 
 Dhamme ṭhito kaññaci ahāpayanto  
  
   Sabbā   vi   Sivi   machasaṃ   Na panappasaṃsaṃ   machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Saggūpagaṃ puññakamamaṃ janinda 
 Mā me tuvaṃ antarāyaṃ akāsi  
 Dadāmi te ummadantiṃ pasatto 
 Rājāva yaññaṃ    dhanaṃ brāhmaṇānaṃ  
      Addhā tuvaṃ katena hitosi mayhaṃ 
 Sakhā mama ummadanti tuvañca  
 Nindeyyu devā pitaro ca sabbe 
 Pāpañca passaṃ abhisamparāyaṃ  
  
      Nahetaṃ dhammaṃ sivirāja vajjuṃ 
 Sanegamā jānapadā ca sabbe  
 Yante mayā ummadanti padintā 
 Bhusehi rājā canathaṃ sajāhi  
      Addhā tuvaṃ katena hitosi mayhaṃ 
 Sakhā mama ummadanti tuvañca  
 Satañca dhammāni sukittitāni  
 Samuddavelāva duraccayāni  
  
                    
      Āhuneyyo mesi hitānukampi 
 Dhātā vidhātā casi kāmapālo  
 Tayi hutā deva mahapphalā hi 
 Kāmena me ummadantiṃ paṭiccha  
  
      Addhā hi sabbaṃ abhipāraka tvaṃ dhammaṃ acāri mama katatupatta  
 Añño nu te ko idha sotthikattā 
 Dipado naro aruṇe jivaloke  
  
      Tuvaṃ nu seṭṭho tvamanuttarosi 
 Tvaṃ dhammagutto dhammavidu sumedho  
 So dhammagutto cirameva jiva 
 Dhammañca me desaya dhammapāla  
  
      Tadiṅgha abhipāraka suṇohi vacanaṃ mama  
 Dhammante desayissāmi sataṃ āsevitaṃ ahaṃ  
  
   Yaññe   ma Cha Saṃ  
  
                    
      Sādhu dhammaruci rājā sādhu paññāṇavā naro  
 Sādhu mittānamaddubbho pāpassākaraṇaṃ sukhaṃ  
  
      Akkodhanassa vijite ṭhitadhammassa rājino  
 Sukhaṃ manussā āsetha sitacchāyāya saṅghare  
  
      Na cāhametaṃ abhirocayāmi 
 Kammaṃ asamekkha kataṃ asādhu  
 Yevāpi ñatvāna sayaṃ karonti 
 Upamā imā myaha tuvaṃ suṇohi  
  
      Gavañce taramānānaṃ jimbhaṃ gacchati puṅgavo  
 Sabbā tā jimbhaṃ gacchanti neteta jimbhaṃ gate sati  
  
      Evameva manussesu yo hoti seṭṭhasammato  
 So ce adhammaṃ carati pageva itarā pajā 
 Sabbaṃ raṭṭhaṃ dukhaṃ seti rājā ce hoti adhammiko  
      Gavañce taramānānaṃ ujuṃ gacchati puṅgavo  
 Sabbā tā ujuṃ gacchanti neteta ujugate sati  
  
      Evameva manussesu yo hoti seṭṭhasammato  
 So cepi dhammaṃ carati pageva itarā pajā 
 Sabbaṃ raṭṭhaṃ sukhaṃ seti rājā ce hoti dhammiko  
                    
      Na cāpahaṃ adhammena amarattamahipatthaye  
 Imaṃ vā paṭhaviṃ sabbaṃ vijetuṃ ahipāraka  
  
      Yaṃ hi kiñci manussesu ratanaṃ idha vijjati  
 Gāvo dāso hiraññañca vatthisaṃ haricandanaṃ  
  
      Assitthiyo ca ratanaṃ maṇikañca 
 Yañcāpi me candasuriyābhipālayanti  
 Na tassa hetu visamaṃ careyya 
 Majjhe sivinaṃ usabhosmi jāto 
  
                    
      Netā pitā uggato raṭṭhapālo 
 Dhammaṃ sivīnaṃ apacāyamāno  
 So dhammamevānuvicintayanto 
 Tasmā sake cittacase na vatte  
  
      Addhā tuvaṃ mahārāja niccaṃ abyasanaṃ sivaṃ  
 Karissasi ciraṃ rajjaṃ paññā hi tava tādisi  
  
      Etaṃ te anumodāmi yaṃ dhammaṃ nappamajjasi  
 Dhammaṃ pamajja khattiyo ṭhānā cavati issaro  
  
      Dhammaṃ cara mahārāja mātāpitusu khattiya  
 Idha dhammaṃ caritvāna rāja saggaṃ gamissasi  
  
      Dhammaṃ cara mahārāja puttadāresu khattiya  
 Idha dhammaṃ caritvāna rāja saggaṃ gamissasi  
  
      Dhammaṃ cara mahārāja mittāmaccesu khattiya  
 Idha dhammaṃ caritvāna rāja saggaṃ gamissasi  
  
      Dhammaṃ cara mahārāja vāhanesu balesu ca  
 Idha dhammaṃ caritvāna rāja saggaṃ gamissasi  
  
      Dhammaṃ cara mahārāja gāmesu nigamesu ca  
 Idha dhammaṃ caritvāna rāja saggaṃ gamissasi  
  
      Dhammaṃ cara mahārāja raṭṭhesu janapadesu ca  
 Idha dhammaṃ caritvāna rāja saggaṃ gamissasi  
  
      Dhammaṃ cara mahārāja samaṇabrāhmaṇesu ca  
 Idha dhammaṃ caritvāna rāja saggaṃ gamissasi  
  
                    
  
      Dhammaṃ cara mahārāja migapakkhīsu khattiya  
 Idha dhammaṃ caritvāna rāja saggaṃ gamissasi  
  
      Dhammaṃ cara mahārāja dhammo ciṇṇo sukhāvaho  
 Idha dhammaṃ caritvāna rāja saggaṃ gamissasi  
  
      Dhammaṃ cara mahārāja saindā sabrahmaka  
 Suciṇṇena divaṃ sattā mā dhammaṃ rāja pamādoti  
 Ummādanti jātakaṃ  
  
   Mahābodhijātakaṃ  
                    
      Kinnu daṇḍaṃ kimajinaṃ kiṃ chattaṃ kiṃ upāhanaṃ  
 Kiṃ aṅkusañca pattañca saṅghāṭiñcāpi brāhmaṇa 
 Taramānarūpo gaṇhāsi kannu patthayase disaṃ  
  
      Dvādasetāni vassāni vusitāni tavantike  
 Nibhājānāmi soṇena piṅgalenābhikujjitaṃ  
      Svāyaṃ dittova nadati sukkadāṭhaṃ vidaṃsayaṃ  
 Tava sutvā sabhariyassa vitasaddhassa maṃ pati  
  
                    
      Ahu esa kato doso yathā bhāsasi brāhmaṇa  
 Esa bhiyyo pasidāmi vasa brāhmaṇa māgamā  
  
      Sabbaseto pure āsi tatopi sabalo ahu  
 Sabbalohitakodāni kālo pakkamituṃ mama  
  
                    
      Abbhantaraṃ pure āsi tato majjhe tato bahi  
 Purā niddhamanā hoti sayameva vajāmahaṃ  
  
      Vitasaddhaṃ na seveyya udapānaṃva nodakaṃ  
 Sacepi naṃ anukhaṇe vārikaddamagandhikaṃ  
  
      Pasantameva seveyya appasannaṃ vivajjaye  
 Pasannaṃ paṭirupāseyya rahadaṃvodakanthiko  
  
      Bhaje bhajantaṃ purisaṃ abhajantaṃ na bhajjaye    
 Asappurisadhammo so yo bhajantaṃ na bhajjati    
  
      Yo bhajantaṃ na bhajati sevamānaṃ na sevati  
 Sa ve manussapāpiṭṭho migo sākhassito yathā  
  
      Accābhikkhaṇasaṃsagagā asamosaraṇena ca  
 Etena mittā jiranti akāle yācanāya ca  
  
      Tasmā nābhikkhaṇaṃ gacche na ca gacche cirāciraṃ  
 Kālena yāvaṃ yāceyya evaṃ mittā na jiyare  
  
      Aticiraṃ nivāsena piyo bhavati appiyo  
 Āmanta kho taṃ gacchāma purā te homa appiyā  
  
                    
      Evaṃ ce    yācamānānaṃ añjaliṃ nāvakhujjhasi  
 Parivārakānaṃ satatānaṃ vacanaṃ na kārosi no 
 Evaṃ taṃ abhiyācāma puna kayirāsi pariyāyaṃ  
  
      Evaṃ ce no viharataṃ antarāyo na hesasti  
 Tumbhaṃ cāpi    mahārāja ambhaṃ    vā raṭṭhavaḍḍhana 
 Appevanāma passema    ahorattānamaccaye  
  
   Nabhaye nabhājaye   vi machasaṃ   Nabhajati   machasaṃ nabhājati   vi 
   Te   machasaṃ   Mayahaṃvā   vi mayahaṃ 
   Tuyahaṃcāpi   vi machasaṃ   Passāma   vi  
  
                    
                    
      Udiraṇā ce saṅgatyā bhāvāya manuvattati  
 Akāmā akaraṇiyaṃ vā karaṇiyaṃ cāpi kubbati 
 Akāmakaraṇiyasmiṃ    kavidha pāpena lippati    
  
      So ce attho ca dhammo ca kalyāṇo na ca pāpako  
 Bhoto ce vacanaṃ saccaṃ suhato vānaro mayā  
  
      Attano ce hi vādassa aparādhaṃ vijāniyā  
 Na maṃ tvaṃ garaheyyāsi bhoto vādo hi tādiso  
  
                    
      Issaro sabbalokassa sace kappeti    jīvitaṃ  
 Iddhibyasanabhāvañca kammaṃ kalyāṇapāpakaṃ 
 Niddesakāri puriso issaro tena lippati  
  
      So ce attho ca dhammo ca kalyāṇo na ca pāpako  
 Bhoto ce vacanaṃ saccaṃ suhato vānaro mayā  
  
      Attano ce hi vādassa aparādhaṃ vijāniyā  
 Na maṃ tvaṃ garaheyyāsi bhoto vādo hi tādiso  
  
      Sace pubbekatahetu sukhadukkhaṃ nigacchati  
 Porāṇakaṃ kataṃ pāpaṃ tameso muñcate iṇaṃ 
 Porāṇakaiṇamokkho kvidha pāpena lippati  
  
                    
      So ce attho ca dhammo ca kalyāṇo na ca pāpako  
 Bhoto ce vacanaṃ saccaṃ suhato vānaro mayā  
  
      Attano ce hi vādassa aparādhaṃ vijāniyā  
 Na maṃ tvaṃ garaheyyāsi bhoto vādo hi tādiso  
   Akāmā karaṇiyamahi   machasaṃ syā   Limpati   machasaṃ syā  
   Kuppeti   machasaṃ 
  
                     
      Catunnaṃyevupādāya rūpaṃ sambhoti pāṇinaṃ  
 Yato ca rūpaṃ sambhoti tattheva    anupagacchati  
  
      Idheva jīvati jivo pecca pecca vinassati  
 Ucchijjati ayaṃ loko ye bālā ye ca paṇḍitā 
 Ucchijjamāne lokasmiṃ kavidha pāpena lippati  
  
      So ce attho ca dhammo ca kalyāṇo na ca pāpako  
 Bhoto ce vacanaṃ saccaṃ suhato vānaro mayā  
  
      Attano ce hi vādassa aparādhaṃ vijāniyā  
 Na maṃ tvaṃ garaheyyāsi bhoto vādo hi tādiso  
  
                    
      Āhu battavidhā loke bālā paṇḍitamānino  
 Mātaraṃ pitaraṃ haññe atho jeṭṭhampi bhātaraṃ 
 Haneyya puttadāre ca attho ce tādiso siyā  
  
      Yassa rukkhassa chāyāya nisideyya sayeyya vā  
 Na tassa sākhaṃ bhañejayya mittadubbho hi pāpako  
  
      Atha attho samuppanne samulamapi abbahe  
 Attho me sambalenāsi suhato vānaro mayā  
  
      So ce attho ca dhammo ca kalyāṇo na ca pāpako  
 Bhoto ce vacanaṃ saccaṃ suhato vānaro mayā  
  
      Attano ce hi vādassa aparādhaṃ vijāniyā  
 Na maṃ tvaṃ garaheyyāsi bhoto vādo hi tādiso  
  
                    
      Ahetuvādo puriso yo ca issarakuttiko  
 Pubbekati ca ucchedi yo ca khattavidho naro 
  
   Tatthevānupa   vi machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Ete asappurisā loke bālā paṇḍitamānino  
 Kareyya tādiso pāpaṃ atho aññampi kāraye 
 Asappurisasaṃsaggo dukkaṭo kaṭukudrayo  
  
      Urabbharūpena khakāsu    pubbe 
 Asaṅkito ajayuthaṃ upeti  
 Hanatvā uraṇiṃ ajiyaṃ    ajañca 
 Citrāsayitvā yena kāmaṃ paleti  
  
                    
      Tathā vidheke samaṇabrāhmaṇāse 
 Chadanaṃ katvā vañcayanti manusse  
 Anāsakā thaṇḍilaseyyakā ca 
 Rajojallaṃ ukkuṭikappadhānaṃ 
 Pariyāyabhantañca apāṇakattaṃ    
 Pāpācārā arahanto vadānā  
  
      Ete asappurisā loke bālā paṇḍitamānino  
 Kareyya tādiso pāpaṃ atho aññampi kāraye 
 Asappurisasaṃsaggo dukkaṭo kaṭukudrayo  
  
      Yamāhu natthi viriyanti hetuñca apavadanti    ye  
 Parakāraṃ attakārañca ye tucchaṃ samavaṇṇayuṃ  
  
      Ete asappurisā loke bālā paṇḍitamānino  
 Kareyya tādiso pāpaṃ atho aññampi kāraye 
 Asappurisasaṃsaggo dukkaṭo    kaṭukudrayo  
  
      Sace hi viriyaṃ nāsasa kammaṃ kalyāṇapāpakaṃ  
 Na bhare vaḍḍhakiṃ    rājā napi yantāni    kāraye  
  
      Yasmā ca viriyaṃ atthi kammaṃ kalyāṇapāpakaṃ  
 Tasmā yantāni kāreti rājā bharati vaḍḍhakiṃ  
  
      Yadi vassasataṃ devo na vasse na himaṃ pate  
 Ucchijjeyya ayaṃ loko vinasseyya ayaṃ pajā  
  
   Vakasusa   machasaṃ vakāsu   vi   Ajikaṃ   machasaṃ   Apāṇakattā   machasaṃ syā   
 Ahetuñca pavadantiye   machasaṃ 
   Dukkhanto   machasaṃ   Vaḍḍhati   machasaṃ   Tantāni   machasaṃ  
  
                    
      Yasmā ca vassati devo himaṃ cāpi   phusiyati  
 Tasmā sassāni paccanti raṭṭhañca pallate viraṃ  
  
      Gamañce taramānānaṃ jimbhaṃ gacchati puṅgavo  
 Sabbā tā jimbhaṃ gacchanti nette jimbhaṃ gate sati  
  
      Evameva manussesu yo hoti seṭṭhasammato  
 So ce adhammaṃ carati pageva itarā pajā 
 Sabbaṃ raṭṭhaṃ dukkhaṃ seti rājā ce hoti adhammiko  
  
      Gamañce taramānānaṃ ujuṃ gacchati puṅgavo  
 Sabbā tā ujuṃ gacchanti nette uju  gate sati 
  
      Evameva manussesu yo hoti seṭṭhasammato  
 So ce dhammaṃ carati pageva itarā pajā 
 Sabbaṃ raṭṭhaṃ dukkhaṃ seti rājā ce hoti adhammiko  
  
      Mahārukkhassa phalino āmaṃ chindati yo phalaṃ  
 Rasañcassa na jānāti bijañcassa vinassati  
  
                    
      Mahārukkhupamaṃ raṭṭhaṃ adhammena yo pasasāsati  
 Rasañcassa na jānāti raṭṭhañcassa vinassati  
  
      Mahārukkhassa phalino pakkaṃ chindati yo phalaṃ  
 Rañcassa vijānāti bijañcassana nassati  
      Mahārukkhupamaṃ raṭṭhaṃ dhammena yo pasāsati  
 Rasañcassa vijāniti raṭṭhañcassa na nassati  
  
      Yoca rājā janapadaṃ adhammena pasāsati  
 Sabbosadhihi so rājā viruddhaṃ hoti khattiyo  
  
   Bhimañcānuphusayati   machasaṃ himaṃcānu phuseyyati   vi   Ujuṃ   machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Tatheva negame hiṃsaṃ ye yuttā kayavikkaye  
 Ojadānabalikāre   sa kosena virujjhati  
  
      Pabhāravarakhettaññu saṅgāme katanissame  
 Ussite hiṃsayaṃ rājā sabalena virujjhati  
  
      Tatheva isayo hiṃsaṃ saṃyame brahmacārino   
 Adhammacāri khattiyo so saggena virujjhati  
  
      Yo ca rājā adhammaṭṭho bhariyaṃ hatta adūsakaṃ  
 Luddaṃ pasavate pāpaṃ   puttehi ca virujjhati  
  
      Dhammañcare jānapade negamesu balesu ca  
 Isayo ca na hiṃseyyaṃ puttadāre samañcare  
      Sa tādiso bhumipati raṭṭhapālo akodhano  
 Sāmante sampakampeti indeva asurādhipoti  
   Mahābodhijātakaṃ 
 Paññāsanipāto niṭṭhito  
 Tassuddānaṃ   
 Sanaḷinikamavhayano paṭhamo 
 Dutiyo pana saummadantivaro  
 Tatiyo pana bodhi sirivhayano 
 Kathitāpana tīṇi jinena subhāti  
  
   Ojadānebalikāre   vi   Brahmacāriye   vi machasaṃ   hānaṃ   machasaṃ syā 
  
                    
 Saṭṭhinipāto 
   Soṇakajātakaṃ 
  
                    
      Kassa sutvā sataṃ dammi sahassaṃ daṭṭhu   soṇakaṃ  
 Ko me soṇaka makkhāti   sahāyaṃ paṃsukiḷitaṃ   
      Atha bravi māṇavako daharo pañcacuḷako  
 Mayhaṃ sutvā sataṃ dehi sahassaṃ daṭṭhu soṇakaṃ 
 Ahaṃ soṇakamakkhissaṃ   sahāyaṃ paṃsukiḷitaṃ 
  
                    
      Katarasmiṃ   so janapade raṭṭhesu nigamesu ca  
 Kattha te soṇako diṭṭho   taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito  
  
      Taveva deva vijite   tavecuyyānabhumiyā  
 Ujuvaṃsā mahāsālā nilobhāsā manoramā 
 Tiṭṭhanti meghasamānā rammā aññoññanissitā  
  
      Tesaṃ mulasmiṃ   soṇako jhāyati anupādano  
 Upādānesu lokesu dayhamānesu   nibbuto  
  
      Tato ca rājā pāyāsi senāya caturaṅgiyā  
 Kārāpetvā samaṃ maggaṃ agamā yena soṇako  
  
      Uyyānabhumiṃ gantvāna vicaranto brahāmane  
 Āsinaṃ soṇakaṃ dakkhi dayhamānesu nibbutaṃ 
  
      Kapaṇovatāyaṃ bhikkhu muṇḍo saṅghāṭipāruto  
 Amātiko apitiko rukkhamulasmiṃ jhāyati  
  
      Imaṃ vākyaṃ nisāmetvā soṇako etadabravi  
 Na rājā kapaṇo hoti dhammaṃ kāyena phassayaṃ  
  
   Diṭṭha   machasaṃ syā   Makkhāsi   machasaṃ   Saha paṃsukiḷitaṃ   vi   
 Soṇakakkhissaṃ   machasaṃ   Katamasmiṃ   machasaṃ   Katthasoṇakamadadakkhi   
 machasaṃ   Jivite   machasaṃ   Mulamhi   machasaṃ   Ḍayahamānesu   vi machasaṃ syā 
  
                    
                    
      Yodha dhammaṃ niraṃkatvā adhammamanuvattati  
 Sa rāja kapaṇo hoti pāpo pāpaparāyano  
  
      Arindamoti me nāmaṃ kāsirājāti maṃ vidu  
 Kacci bhoto sukhaseyyā idha pattassa soṇaka 
  
      Sadāpi bhadumadhanassa anāgārassa bhikkhuno  
 Na tesaṃ koṭṭhe openti na kumbhiṃ na kaḷopiyaṃ 
 Paraniṭṭhita   mesānā tena yāpenati subbatā  
  
      Dutiyampi bhadumadhanassa anāgārassa bhikkhuno  
 Anavajjapiṇḍo bhottabbo na ca kocuparodhati  
  
      Tatiyampi bhadumadhanassa anāgārassa bhikkhuno  
 Nibbuta  piṇḍo bhottabbo na ca kocuparodhati  
  
      Catutthampi bhadumadhanassa anāgārassa bhikkhuno  
 Muttassa raṭṭhe carato saṅgho yassa na vijjati  
      Pañcampi bhadumadhanassa anāgārassa bhikkhuno  
 Nagarambhi dayhamānamhi nāssa kiñci adayhatha  
                    
      Chaṭṭhampi bhadumadhanassa anāgārassa bhikkhuno  
 Raṭṭhe vilumpamānamhi nāssa kiñci ahāratha  
      Sattamampi bhadumadhanassa anāgārassa bhikkhuno  
 Corehi rakkhitaṃ maggaṃ ye caññe paripatthikā pattacivaramādāya sotthiṃ gacchati subbato  
  
      Aṭṭhamampi bhadumadhanassa anāgārassa bhikkhuno  
 Yaṃ yaṃ disaṃ pakakamati anapekkhova gacchati  
   Paritiṭṭhita   vi machasaṃ syā   Nibbuto   vi machasaṃ   Āharatha   machasaṃ 
  
                    
                    
      Bahuni   samaṇabhaduni ye tvaṃ bhikkhu pasaṃsasi  
 Ahañca giddho kāmesu kathaṃ kāhāmi soṇaka 
  
      Piyā me mānusā kāmā atho dibyāpi   me piyā  
 Atha kena nu vaṇṇena abho loke labhambhase  
  
                    
      Kāmesu giddhā kāmaratā kāmesu adhimucchitā  
 Narā pāpāni katvāna upapajjanti duggatiṃ 
  
      Ye ca kāme pahatvāna nikkhantā akutobhayā  
 Ekodibhāvādhigatā na te gacchanti duggatiṃ  
  
      Upamante karissāmi taṃ suṇohi arandama  
 Upamāyapidhekacce   atthaṃ jānanti paṇḍitā 
  
      Gaṅgāya kuṇapaṃ disvā cuyhamānaṃ mahaṇṇave  
 Vāyaso samavintesi appapañño acetaso 
  
      Yānañca vatidaṃ laddhaṃ bhakkhovāyaṃ anapapako  
 Tattha rattiṃ tattha divā tattheva nirato mano  
  
      Khādaṃ nāgassa maṃsāni picaṃ bhāgirathodakaṃ  
 Sampassaṃ vanacetyāni na palettha   vihaṅgamo  
  
      Tañca otaraṇi gaṅgā pamatataṃ kuṇape rataṃ  
 Samuddaṃ ajjhagāhāsi agati yattha pakkhinaṃ  
  
      So ca bhakkhaparikkhiṇo uppatitvā   vihaṅgamo  
 Na pacchato na purato nuttaraṃ nopi dakkhiṇaṃ  
  
      Dīpaṃ so na ajjhagañchi agati yattha pakkhinaṃ  
 So ca tattheva pāpattha yathā dubbalako tathā  
  
   Bahu pi bhadrā etesaṃ   machasaṃ bahupi bhadrakā ete   vi   Dibbāpi   vi   Upamāya 
 vidhekacce   machasaṃ   Napaḷetha   machasaṃ   Upadatvā   vi machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Tañca sāmuddikā macchā kumahilā makarā susu  
 Pasayhakārā khādiṃsu endamānaṃ vipakkhinaṃ   
  
      Evameva tuvaṃ rāja ye caññe kāmabhogino  
 Giddhā ce na vamissanti kākapaññāya   te vidu  
  
      Esā te upamā rāja atthasandassani katā  
 Tvaṃ ca paññāyase tena yadi kāhasi vā na vā  
  
                    
      Ekavācampi dve vācaṃ bhaṇeyya anukampako  
 Tatuttariṃ   na bhāseyya dāso vayyassa   sannike  
  
      Idaṃ vatvāna pakkāmi soṇako amitabuddhimā  
 Vehāse antalikkhasmiṃ anusāsitvāna khattiyaṃ  
  
                    
      Ko nu me rājakattāro sutā ceyyattimāgatā   
 Rajjaṃ niyyādayissāmi nāhaṃ rajjenamatthiko  
  
      Ajjeva pabbajissāmi ko jaññā maraṇaṃ suve  
 Māhaṃ kākova dummedho kāmānaṃ vasamanacagaṃ 
  
      Atthi te daharo putto dighāvu raṭṭhavaḍḍhano  
 Taṃ rajje abhisiñcassu so no rājā bhavissati  
  
      Khippaṃ kumāraṃ ānetha dighāvuṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhanaṃ  
 Taṃ rājje abhisiñcissaṃ so vo rājā bhavissati  
  
      Tato kumāraṃ ānesuṃ dighāvuṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhanaṃ  
 Taṃ disvā ālapi rājā ekaputtaṃ manoramaṃ  
  
      Saṭṭhi gāmasahassāni paripuṇṇāni sabbaso  
 Te putta paṭipajjassu rajjaṃ niyyādayāmi te 
  
   Vipakkhakaṃ   machasaṃ   Kākapaññāca   machasaṃ   Taduttari   machasaṃ   Ayiyassa 
   vi   Sudadāveyyattamāgatā   machasaṃ suduveyyatati māgatā   vi 
  
                    
      Ajjeva pabbajissāmi ko jaññā maraṇaṃ suve  
 Māhaṃ kākova dummedho kāmānaṃ vasamānacagaṃ 
  
      Saṭṭhināgasahassani sabbālaṅkārabhusitā  
 Suvaṇṇakacchā mātaṅgā hemakappanavāsasā  
  
      Ārūḷhā gāmaṇiyehi tomaraṅkusapāṇihi  
 Te putta paṭipajjassu rajjaṃ niyyādayāmi te  
  
      Ajjeva pabbajissāmi ko jaññā maraṇaṃ suve  
 Māhaṃ kākova dummedho kāmānaṃ vasamanavagaṃ 
  
      Saṭṭhiassasahassāni sabbālaṅkārabhusitā  
 Ājāniyā ca jātiyā sindhavā sighavāhanaṃ 
  
      Ārūḷhā gāmaṇiyehi tomaraṅkusapāṇihi  
 Te putta paṭipajjassu rajjaṃ niyyādayāmi te  
      Ajjeva pabbajissāmi ko jaññā maraṇaṃ suve  
 Māhaṃ kākova dummedho kāmānaṃ vasamanavagaṃ 
  
                    
      Saṭṭhiassasahassāni sannaddhā ussitaddhajā  
 Dipā athopi veyyagghā   sabbālaṅkārabhusitā 
  
      Ārūḷhā gāmaṇiyehi cāpahatthehi vammihi  
 Te putta paṭipajjassu rajjaṃ niyyādayāmi te  
  
      Ajjeva pabbajissāmi ko jaññā maraṇaṃ suve  
 Māhaṃ kākova dummedho kāmānaṃ vasamanavagaṃ 
  
      Saṭṭhiassasahassāni rohaññā suṅgavusabhā  
 Tā putta paṭipajjassu rajjaṃ niyyādayāmi te  
  
      Ajjeva pabbajissāmi ko jaññā maraṇaṃ suve  
 Māhaṃ kākova dummedho kāmānaṃ vasamanvagaṃ  
  
      Soḷasitthisahassāni sabbālaṅkārabhusitā  
 Vicitravatthābharaṇā āmuttamaṇikuṇḍalā 
 Tā putta paṭipajjassu rajjaṃ niyyādayāmi te  
  
   Veyagghaṃ   machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Ajjeva pabbajissāmi ko jaññā maraṇaṃ suve  
 Māhaṃ kākova dummedho kāmānaṃ vasamanavagaṃ 
  
      Daharasseva me tāta mātā matāti me sutaṃ  
 Tayā vinā ahaṃ tāta jīvitumpi na ussahe  
  
      Yathā āraññakaṃ nāgaṃ poto anveti pacchato  
 Jessantaṃ   giriduggesu samesu visamesu ca  
  
      Evaṃ taṃ anugacchāmi puttamādāya gacchato  
 Subharo te bhavissāmi na te hessāmi dubbharo  
  
      Yathā sāmuddikaṃ nāvaṃ vāṇijānaṃ dhanesinaṃ  
 Vohāro tattha gaṇheyya vāṇijā byasani   siyā  
  
      Imaṃ kumāraṃ pāpetha pāsādaṃ rativaḍḍhanaṃ  
                    
 Tattha kambusahatthāyo yathā sakkaṃva accharā 
 Tā naṃ tattha ramessanti tāhi ceso ramissati  
  
      Tato kumāraṃ pāpesuṃ pāsādaṃ rativaḍḍhanaṃ  
 Taṃ disvā avacuṃ   kaññā dighāvuṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhanaṃ  
  
      Devatānusi gandhabbo ādu sakko purindado  
 Ko vā tvaṃ kassa vā putto kathaṃ jānemu taṃ mayaṃ  
  
      Namhi devo na gandhabbo napi   sakko purindado  
 Kāsi rañño ahaṃ putto dighāvu raṭṭhavaḍḍhano 
 Mamaṃ bharatha bhaddaṃ vo   ahaṃ bhattā bhavāmi vo  
  
      Taṃ tattha avacuṃ kaññā dighāvuṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhanaṃ  
 Kuhiṃ rā anuppetto ito rājā kuhiṃ gato  
  
   Desasantaṃ   machasaṃ   Byasanaṃ   machasaṃ   Evamevāyaṃputatakali   vi machasaṃ 
   Avacaṃ   machasaṃ   Namhi   machasaṃ   Te   machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Paṅkaṃ rājā atikkanto thale rājā patiṭṭhito  
 Akaṇṭakaṃ agahanaṃ paṭipanno mahāpathaṃ  
  
      Ahañca paṭipannosmi maggaṃ duggatigāminaṃ sakaṇṭakaṃ sagahanaṃ yena 
 gacchanti   duggatiṃ  
  
      Tassa te svāgataṃ rājā sihassova giribbajaṃ  
 Anusāsa mahārāja tvaṃ no sabbāsamissaroti  
 Soṇakajātakaṃ  
  
   Saṅkiccajātakaṃ                    
      Disvā nisinnaṃ rājānaṃ brahmadantaṃ rathesabhaṃ  
 Athassa paṭivedesi yassāsi anukampako 
  
      Saṅkiccāyaṃ anuppatto isinaṃ sādhusammato  
 Taramānarūpo niyyāhi khippaṃ passa mahesinaṃ 
  
      Tato ca rājā tararamāno yuttamāruyha sandanaṃ  
 Mittāmaccaparibbuḷho agamāsi rathesabho  
  
      Nikkhippa   pañca kakudhāni kāsinaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhano  
 Vāḷavijanimuṇhīsaṃ khaggaṃ chattañcupāhanaṃ  
  
      Oruyha rājā yānambhā ṭhapayitvā   pacchadaṃ  
 Āsinaṃ dāyapassasmiṃ saṅkiccamupasaṅkami  
  
      Upasaṅkamitvā so rājā sammodi isinā saha taṃ kathaṃ vitisāretvā ekamantaṃ upāvisi  
  
      Ekamantaṃ nisinnova atha kālaṃ amaññatha  
 Tato pāpāni kammāni pucchituṃ paṭipajjatha  
  
   Gacchāmi   vi Machasaṃ   Nikkhipa   machasaṃ   Thapayitvā   machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Isiṃ pucchāmi   saṅkiccaṃ isinaṃ sādhusammataṃ  
 Āsinaṃ dāyapassasmiṃ isisaṅghapurakkhataṃ   
  
                    
      Kaṃ gatiṃ pepacca   gacchanti narā dhammāticārino  
 Aticiṇṇo mayā dhammo tamme akkhāhi pucchito  
  
      Isi avaca saṅkicco kāsinaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhanaṃ  
 Āsinaṃ dāyapassasmiṃ mahārāja suṇohi me  
      Uppathena vajantassa yo maggamanusāsati  
 Tassa ce vacanaṃ kayirā nāssa maggeyya kaṇṭako  
  
      Adhammaṃ paṭipannassa yo dhammamanusāsati  
 Tassa te vacanaṃ kayirā na so gaccheya duggatiṃ  
  
                    
      Dhammo patho mahārāja adhammo pana uppatho  
 Adhammo nirayaṃ neti dhammo pāpeti suggatiṃ  
  
      Adhammacārino rāja narā visamajivino  
 Yaṃ gatiṃ pecca gacchanti niraye te suṇohi me  
  
      Sañachivo kāḷasutto ca saṅghāto   dve ca roruvā  
 Athāparo mahāvici tapano ca patāpano  
  
      Iccete aṭṭha nirayā akkhātā duratikkamā  
 Ākiṇṇā luddakammehi paccekā soḷasussadā  
      Kadariyatāpanā ghorā accimanto mabhabbhāyā  
 Lomahaṃsanarūpā ca bhesmā paṭibhayā dukhā  
  
   Pucchāma   syā   Purakkhitaṃ   machasaṃ   Pacca   machasaṃ   Saṅghāṭo   machasaṃ 
      
  
                    
      Catukkaṇṇā catudvārā vibhattā bhāgaso mitā  
 Ayopākārapariyantā ayasā paṭikujjitā  
  
      Tesaṃ ayomayā bhūmi jalitā tejasā yutā  
 Samantā yojanasataṃ phuṭā tiṭṭhanti sabbadā  
  
      Ete pattani niraye uddhapādā avaṃsirā  
 Isīnaṃ ativattāro saññatānaṃ tapassinaṃ  
  
      Te bhūnahuno paccanti macchā bilakatā yathā  
 Saṃvacchare asaṅkheyye narā kibbisakārino  
  
      Dayha    mānena gattena niccaṃ santarabāhiraṃ  
 Nirayā nādigacchanti dvāraṃ nikkhamanesino  
  
      Puratthimena dhāvanti tato dhāvanti pacchato  
 Uttarenapi dhāvanti tato dhāvanti dakkhiṇaṃ  
  
      Yaṃ yaṃ hi dvāraṃ gacchanti taṃ tadeva pithiyati    
                    
 Bahunivassasahassāni    janā nirayagāmino    
 Bāhā paggayha nandanti patvā dukkhaṃ anappakaṃ  
  
      Āsivisaṃva kupitaṃ    tejassiṃ    duratikkamaṃ  
 Na sādhurūpe āside saññatānaṃ tapassanaṃ  
  
      Atikāyo mahisasāso ājjuno kekakādhipo    
 Sahassabāhu ucchinno    isimāsajja gotamaṃ  
  
      Arajaṃ rajasā vacchaṃ kisaṃ avakiriya daṇḍakī  
 Talova mulato    chinto sarājā vibhavaṅgato  
  
      Upahacca manaṃ mejjho     mātaṅgasmiṃ yassasine  
 Sapārisajjo ucchānno mejjhāraññaṃ     tadā ahu  
  
   Ḍayaha   vi machasaṃ   Pidhiyare   machasaṃ   Bahutisatasahassāni   vi machasaṃ 
   Vāsino   vi   Kuppitaṃ   machasaṃ   Tejasiṃ   vi machasaṃ 
   Ketakādhipo   vi machasaṃ   Acchinno   machasaṃ   Mulako   machasaṃ 
    Majjho   machasaṃ    Majjhāraññaṃ   machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Kaṇhādipāyanāsajja isiṃ andhakaveṇhuyo  
 Aññamaññaṃ musale    hanatvā sampannā yamasādhanaṃ  
  
      Athāyaṃ isinā satto antalikkhe caro pure  
 Pāvekkhi paṭhaviṃ    cecco hīnatto pattapariyāyaṃ  
  
      Tasmā hi chandāgamanaṃ nappasaṃsanti paṇḍitā  
 Aduṭṭhacitto bhāseyya giraṃ saccupasaṃhitaṃ  
  
      Manasā ce paduṭṭhena yo naro pekkhate muniṃ  
 Vijjāvaraṇasampannaṃ gantā so nirayaṃ adho  
  
      Ye muddhe    paribhāsanti pharusupakkamā janā  
 Anapaccā adāyādā tālavatthu bhavanta  
      Yo ca pabbajitaṃ    hanti katakiccaṃ mahesinaṃ  
 Sa kāḷasuteta niraye cirarattāya paccati  
  
      Yo ca rājā adhammaṭṭho raṭṭhaviddhaṃsano    cuto  
 Tāpayitvā janapadaṃ tāpane pecca    paccati  
  
      Yo ca vassasahassānaṃ    sataṃ dibyāni    paccati  
 Acacisaṅghapareto so dukkhaṃ vedeti vedanaṃ  
  
                    
      Tassa aggisikhā kāyā niccharanti pabhassarā  
 Tejobhakkhassa gattāni lomaggehi nakhehi ca  
  
      Dayha    mānena gattena niccaṃ santarabāhiraṃ     
 Dukkhāhitunto nadati nāgo tuttaddito     yathā  
  
      Yo lohā pitaraṃ hanti dosā vā purisādhamo  
 Sa kāḷasutte niraye cirarattāya paccati  
  
   Musalā   machasaṃ   Pathaviṃ   machasaṃ   Vuḍḍhe   machasaṃ 
   Pabbajjitaṃ   machasaṃ   Raṭṭhadhaṃsano   vi machasaṃ   Pacca   machasaṃ 
   Vassasahassāni   machasaṃ   Dibbāni   machasaṃ   Ḍayha   vi machasaṃ 
    Antara   machasaṃ    Tutataṭṭito   machasaṃ tuṇḍaṭaṭito   syā  
  
                    
      Sa tāsiso paccati lohakumbhiyaṃ 
 Pakkañca santihi hananti nittacaṃ  
 Andhaṃ karitvā muttakarisabhakkhaṃ 
 Khāre    nimujjenti tathāvidhaṃ naraṃ  
  
      Tantaṃ pakkaṭṭhitaṃ    ayoguḷañca 
 Dīghe ca phāle cirarattatāpite  
 Vikkhambhamādāya vihajja rajjuhi 
 Vivaṭe mukhe saṃsavayanti    rakkhasā  
  
      Sāmā ca soṇā sabalā ca gijjha 
 Kākoḷasaṅghā ca dijā ayomukhā  
 Saṅgamma khādanti vipphandamānaṃ  
 Jivhaṃ vibhajja    vighāsaṃ    salohitaṃ  
  
      Taṃ daḍḍhatālaṃ paribhinnagattaṃ 
 Nipphoṭhayantā    anuvicaranti rakkhasā  
 Rati hi tesaṃ dukhino panitare 
 Etādisasmiṃ niraye vasanti 
 Ye keci loke idha pettighātino 
  
      Putto ca mātaraṃ hanatvā ito gantvā yamakkhayaṃ  
 Bhusamāpajjate dukkhaṃ attakammaphalūpago  
  
      Amanussā atibalā    hantāraṃ janayantiyā  
 Ayomayehi vālehi piḷayanti punappunaṃ  
  
                    
      Taṃ passavaṃ    sakā gatatā rudhiraṃ   attasambhavaṃ  
 Tambalohavilinaṃva     tattaṃ pāyenti mattiyaṃ  
  
      Jigucchaṃ kuṇapaṃ puti duggandhaṃ     guthakadadmaṃ  
 Pubbalohitasaṅkāsaṃ rahadaṃ     ogayha tiṭṭhati  
  
      Tamenaṃ kimayo tattha atikāyā ayomukhā  
 Chaviṃ chetvāna khādanti pagiddhā maṃsalohite  
  
      So ca taṃ nirayaṃ patto nimuggo sataporisaṃ  
 Putikaṃ kuṇapaṃ vāti samantā satayojanaṃ  
  
   Māde   Asibalā   machasaṃ 
   Pakkuṭṭhitamayoguḷañca   machasaṃ   Tamassavaṃ   machasaṃ 
   Saṃpavisanti   machasaṃ   Ruhiraṃ   vi 
   Vihiṃja   machasaṃ    Tamabalohavilinanaṃva   machasaṃ 
   Vighāsaṃva   machasaṃ    Dugandhaṃ   machasaṃ 
   Nippothayantā   syā    Rabhadavoggassa   machasaṃ rabhadoggayha   syā  
                    
      Cakkhumāpi hi cakkhuhi tena gandhena jiyati etādisaṃ brahmadanta mātughāti    
 labhe dukhaṃ  
  
      Khuradhāramanukkamma tikkhaṃ durabhisambhavaṃ  
 Patanti gabbhapātiniyo    duggaṃ vetaraṇiṃ nadiṃ  
  
      Ayomayā simbaliyo soḷasaṅgulakaṇṭakā  
 Ubhato mahilambanti duggaṃ teraṇiṃ nadiṃ  
  
      Te accimanto tiṭṭhanti aggikkhandhāva ārakā  
 Ādintā jātavedena uddhaṃ yojanamuggatā  
  
      Ete sajanti niraye tatte tikhiṇakaṇṭake  
 Nāriyo ca aticāriṇiyo    narā ca paradāragū  
  
      Te patanti adhokkhandhā    vivattā    vihatā puthu  
 Sayanti vinividdhaṅgā dīghaṃ jagganti saṃvariṃ  
  
      Tato ratyā vivasane mahatiṃ pabbatupamaṃ  
 Lohakumbhiṃ pavajjanti tattaṃ aggisamudakaṃ  
  
      Evaṃ divā ca ratto ca dusasilā mohapārutā  
 Anubhonti sakaṃ kammaṃ pubbe dukkatamatatano  
  
      Yā ca bhariyā dhanakkitā sāmikaṃ atimaññati sassuṃ vā sasuraṃ vāpi jeṭṭhaṃ vāpi 
 nanandaraṃ    
  
      Tassā vaṅkena jivhaggaṃ nibbahanti sabandhanaṃ  
                    
 Sabyāmamattaṃ kiminaṃ jivhaṃ pasasti antano 
 Viññāpetuṃ sakkoti tāpane pecca    paccati  
  
   Mātuḷolate dukhaṃ   machasaṃ syā mattigho   vi 
   Gabbhapātiyo   machasaṃ   Ativārā   machasaṃ aticāri   vi 
   Adhakkhandhā   machasaṃ vi   Vigattā   machasaṃ 
   Nandanaṃ   syā machasaṃ   Sacca   machasaṃ  
  
                    
      Orabbhikā sukarikā macchikā migabandhakā  
 Corā goghātakā luddā avaṇṇe vaṇṇakārākā  
  
      Sattihi lobhakūṭehi nettiṃsehi usuhi ca  
 Haññamānā khāranadiṃ papatanti    avaṃsirā  
  
      Sāyaṃ pāto kūṭakāri ayokuṭehi haññati  
 Tato vantaṃ durattānaṃ paresaṃ buñajate    sadā  
  
      Dhaṅkā bheraṇḍakā    gijjhā kākoḷā ca ayomukhā  
 Vipphandamānaṃ    khādanti naraṃ kibbisakārinaṃ  
  
      Ye vigena migaṃ hanti pakkhiṃ vā pana pakkhinā  
 Asanto rajasā channā gantā te nirayussadaṃ 
  
                    
      Santo ca uddhaṃ gacchanti suviṇṇenidha kamamunā  
 Suciṇṇassa phalaṃ passa sahindā devā sabuhmakā  
  
      Taṃ taṃ brūmi mahārāja dhammaṃ raṭṭhapati cara  
 Tathā    tathā rāja carāhi dhammaṃ 
 Yathā taṃ suciṇṇaṃ nānutappeyya pacchāti  
 Saṅkicca jātakaṃ  
  
 Saṭṭhinipātaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ 
 Tassuddānaṃ  
 Atha saṭṭhinipātamhi suṇātha mama bhāsitaṃ pavaro soṇaka arindamasambhayano 
 Tathā vutta rathesabha kicca varoti  
  
   Saṃpatanti   machasaṃ   Bhuñjare   machasaṃ   Bhedaṇaṃḍakā   machasaṃ 
   Vipandamānaṃ   vi   Tathārāja   machasaṃ 
  
                    
 Sattatinipāto 
   Kusajātakaṃ  
          
      Idaṃ te raṭṭhaṃ sadhanaṃ sayoggaṃ 
 Sakāyuraṃ sabbakāmūpapannaṃ  
 Idante rajjaṃ anusāsa amma 
 Gacchāmahaṃ yattha piyā pabhāvati  
  
                    
      Anujajubhutena haraṃ mahantaṃ    
 Divā ca ratto ca nisithakāle    
 Paṭigaccha tvaṃ khippaṃ kusāvatiṃ kusa 
 Na icchāmi    dubbaṇṇamahaṃ vasantaṃ  
  
                    
      Nāhaṃ gamissāmi ito kusāvatiṃ 
 Pabhāvati vaṇṇapalohito tava  
 Ramāmi maddasasa niketaramme 
 Hitvāna raṭṭhaṃ tava dassane rato  
  
      Pabhāvati vaṇṇapalohito tava 
 Sammuḷharūpo vicarāmi mediniṃ  
 Disaṃ na jānāmi kutombhi āgato 
 Tayambhi matto migamandalocane  
  
      Suvaṇṇacīravasane jātarūpasumekhale  
 Sussoṇi    tava kāmā hi nāhaṃ rajjenamatthiko  
  
                    
      Abbhu hi tassa bho hoti yo anicchantamicchati  
 Akāmaṃ rāja kāmehi akanto kanta    micchasi  
  
      Akāmaṃ vā sakāmaṃ vā yo naro labhate piyaṃ  
 Lābhamettha pasaṃsāmi    alābho tattha pāpako  
  
   Mahanti   machasaṃ   Nisidakāle   machasaṃ   Nicchāmi   machasaṃ 
   Susoṇi   machasaṃ   Kantu   machasaṃ   Pasaṃsāma   machasaṃ vi  
  
                    
      Pāsāṇasāraṃ khaṇasi kaṇikārassa dārunā  
 Vātaṃ jālena bādhesi yo anicchantamicchati  
      Pāsāṇo nūna te bhadaye ohito mudulakkhaṇe  
 Yo te sātaṃ na vindāmi tirojanapadāgato 
  
                    
      Yadā maṃ bhūkuṭiṃ    katvā rājaputti udikkhasi  
 Āḷāriko tadā homi rañño maddassa    thipure  
  
      Yadā umbhayamānā maṃ rājaputti udikkhasi  
 Nāḷāriko tadā homi rājā bhomi tadā kuso  
  
      Sace hi vacanaṃ saccaṃ nemittānaṃ bhavissati  
 Neva me tvaṃpati assa kāmaṃ chidantu sattadhā  
      Sace hi vacanaṃ saccaṃ aññesaṃ yadi vā mama  
 Neva tuyhaṃ pati atthi añño sihassarā kusā  
  
                    
      Nekkhaṃ    givante kāressa patvā khujje kusavātiṃ  
 Sace maṃ nāganāsuru olokeyya pabhāvati  
  
      Nekkhaṃ givante kāressaṃ   patvā khujje kusavātiṃ  
 Sace maṃ nāganāsuru   ālapeyya pabhāvati  
  
      Nekkhaṃ givante kāressaṃ patvā khujje kusavātiṃ  
 Sace maṃ nāganāsuru umbhāyeyya    pabhāvati  
  
      Nekkhaṃ givante kāressaṃ patvā khujje kusavātiṃ  
 Sace maṃ nāganāsuru pambhāyeyya    pabhāvati  
  
      Nekkhaṃ givante kāressaṃ patvā khujje kusavātiṃ  
 Sace maṃ nāganāsuru pāṇihi    upasamphuse   
  
   Bhukuṭikaṃ   vi   Dadassante   machasaṃ   Nikkhaṃ   machasaṃ 
   Kārissaṃ   machasaṃ   Anāganāsuraṃ   machasaṃ syā nāganāsuraṃ   vi  
   Umbhāpeyya   vi machasaṃ   Pambhāpeyya   vi machasaṃ   Pāṇinā   machasaṃ  
  
                    
                    
      Nahi nunāyaṃ rājaputti rājaputti kuse sātampi vindati  
 Āḷārike bhate    pose vetanena    anatthike  
  
                    
      Nahi nūna    ayaṃ khujjā labhati jivihāya chedanaṃ  
 Sunisitena satthena evaṃ dubbhāsitaṃ bhaṇaṃ  
  
      Mā naṃ rūpena pāmesi ārohena pabhāvati  
 Mahāyasoti katvāna karassu rucire piyaṃ 
  
      Mā naṃ rūpena pāmesi ārohena pabhāvati  
 Mahaddhanoti katvāna karassu rucire piyaṃ 
  
      Mā naṃ rūpena pāmesi ārohena pabhāvati  
 Mahabbaloti katvāna karassu rucire piyaṃ 
  
      Mā naṃ rūpena pāmesi ārohena pabhāvati  
 Mahāraṭṭhoti katvāna karassu rucire piyaṃ 
  
      Mā naṃ rūpena pāmesi ārohena pabhāvati  
 Mahārājāti katvāna karassu rucire piyaṃ 
  
      Mā naṃ rūpena pāmesi ārohena pabhāvati  
 Sīhassaroti katvāna karassu rucire piyaṃ 
      Mā naṃ rūpena pāmesi ārohena pabhāvati  
 Vaggussaroti katvāna karassu rucire piyaṃ 
  
      Mā naṃ rūpena pāmesi ārohena pabhāvati  
 Bindussaroti katvāna karassu rucire piyaṃ 
  
      Mā naṃ rūpena pāmesi ārohena pabhāvati  
 Mañjussaroti katvāna karassu rucire piyaṃ 
  
   Bhaṭe   machasaṃ   Vettanena   machasaṃ   Nunāyaṃ sā khujjā   machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Mā naṃ rūpena pāmesi ārohena pabhāvati  
 Madhurassaroti katvāna karassu rucire piyaṃ 
  
      Mā naṃ rūpena pāmesi ārohena pabhāvati  
 Satasippoti katvāna karassu rucire piyaṃ 
  
      Mā naṃ rūpena pāmesi ārohena pabhāvati  
 Khattiyoti katvāna karassu rucire piyaṃ 
  
      Mā naṃ rūpena pāmesi ārohena pabhāvati  
 Kusarājāti katvāna karassu rucire piyaṃ 
  
                    
      Ete nālā upatthaddhā sabbe tiṭṭhanti vammitā  
 Purā maddanti pākāraṃ ānentetaṃ pabhāvatiṃ  
  
      Satta khaṇḍe    karitvāna ahametaṃ pabhāvatiṃ  
 Khantiyānaṃ padassāmi ye maṃ hattumidhāgatā  
  
      Athuṭṭhuhī rājaputti sāmā koseyyavāsini  
 Assupuṇṇehi nettehi dāsigaṇapurakkhatā  
  
                    
      Taṃ nūna kakkupasevitaṃ mukhaṃ 
 Ādāsadantā tharupaccavekkhitaṃ  
 Subhaṃ sunteṃ virajaṃ anaṅgaṇaṃ 
 Chuddhaṃ vane ṭhassati khantiyehi  
  
      Te nūna me asite vellitagge 
 Kese mudu candanasāralitte  
 Samākule sivathikāya    majjhe 
 Pādehi gijjhā parikaḍḍhayanti    
  
      Tā nūna me tambatakhā sulomā 
 Bāhā mudu candanasāralittā  
 Channā vane ujjhitā khantiyehi  
 Gayha dhaṅko gacchati yenakāmaṃ  
  
   Khile   machasaṃ   Sivaṭhikāya   machasaṃ   Parikaḍḍhiyanti   machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Te nūna tālupanibhe alambe 
 Nisevite kāsikacandanena  
 Thanesu me lambisasti sigālo    
 Mātāva putto taruṇo tanujo  
  
      Taṃ nūna soṇiṃ puthulaṃ sukoṭṭhitaṃ 
 Nisevitaṃ kañcana mekhalāhi    
 Chinnaṃ vane khantiyehi avatthaṃ  
 Sigālasaṅghā parikaḍḍhayanti    
  
      Soṇā dhaṅkā sigālā ca ye caññe santi dāṭhino  
 Ajarā nūna hessanti bhakkhayitvā pabhāvatiṃ  
  
      Sace maṃsāni bhāresuṃ    khantiyā duragāmino  
 Aṭṭhini amma yācitvā anupanthe    ahātha naṃ  
  
      Khentāni amma kāretvā kaṇikārettha ropaya  
 Yadā te puppitā assu hemantānaṃ himaccaye 
 Sareyyātha mamaṃ amma evaṃvaṇṇā pabhāvati  
  
                    
      Tassā mātā udaṭṭhāsi khattiyā devavaṇṇinī  
 Disvā asiñca suṇañca rañño maddassa thipure  
  
                    
      Iminā nūna asinā susaññaṃ tanumajjhimaṃ  
 Dhitaraṃ mama hanatvāna    khantiyānaṃ padassasi  
  
      Na me akāsi vacanaṃ atthakāmāya puttike  
 Sājja lohitasaññachantā gañachisi    yamasādhanaṃ  
  
      Evamāpajjati poso pāpiyaññaca nigacchati  
 Yo ve hitānaṃ vacanaṃ na karaṃ atthadassinaṃ  
  
      Sace tvaṃ amma dhāresi    kumāraṃ cārudassanaṃ  
 Kusena jātaṃ khattiyaṃ suvaṇṇamaṇimekhalaṃ 
 Pujitaṃ ñātisaghehi na gañchisi yamakkhayaṃ  
  
      Yatthassu bherī nadati kuñajaro paṭikujjati    
 Khattiyānaṃ kule bhadde kinnu sukhataraṃ tato  
  
   Diṅgālo   vi machasaṃ   Dhitaraṃ madadahanatvāna 
   Mekhalehi   machasaṃ   Gacchasi   machasaṃ 
   Gayhāvako gacchati yena kāma   vi   Saceva ajjadhāresi   machasaṃ 
   Bhariṃsu   machasaṃ   Kañajaroca nikujati   vi machasaṃ syā 
   Anupathe   machasaṃ  
                    
      Asso hasisati dvāre kumāro uparodati  
 Khattiyānaṃ kule bhadde kinnu sukhataraṃ tato  
  
      Mayurakoñcāhirude kokilābhinikujite  
 Khantiyānaṃ kule bhadde kinnu sukhataraṃ tato  
  
                    
      Kahaṃ nukho sattumaddano pararaṭṭhappamaddano  
 Kuso soḷārapaññāṇo so no dukkhā pamocaye  
  
      Idheva so sattumaddano    pararaṭṭhappamaddano  
 Kuso soḷārapaññāṇo yo no dukkhā    pamocaye  
  
      Ummattikā nu bhanasi ādu bālāva    bhāsasi  
 Kuso ce āgato assa kiṃ na jānemu taṃ mayaṃ  
  
                    
      Eso āḷāriko poso kumāripuramantare  
 Daḷhaṃ katvāna saṃvelliṃ    kumbhiṃ dhovati onato 
  
      Veṇi tvamasi caṇḍāli ādusi kulagandhinī  
 Kathaṃ maddakule jātā dasaṃ kayirāsi kāmukaṃ  
  
      Nambhi veṇi na vaṇḍāli na cambhi kulagandhinī  
 Okkākaputto bhaddante tvannu dāsoti maññasi  
  
      Yo brāhmaṇasahassāni sadā bhojeti visatiṃ  
 Okkākaputto bhaddante tvannu dāsoti maññasi  
  
                    
      Yassa nāgasahassāni sadā bhojenti visatiṃ  
 Okkākaputto bhaddante tvannu dāsoti maññasi  
  
   Sattumadāno   machasaṃ   Sabbe vadhissati   machasaṃ   Andhabālā   machasaṃ 
 Andhabālā pabhāssi   syā   Saṃvellaṃ   machasaṃ syā  
  
                    
  
      Yassa assasahassāni sadā bhojenti visatiṃ  
 Okkākaputto bhaddante tvannu dāsoti maññasi  
  
      Yassa rathasahassāni sadā yojenti visatiṃ  
 Okkākaputto bhaddante tvannu dāsoti maññasi  
  
      Yassa usabhasasahassāni sadā yojenti visatiṃ  
 Okkākaputto bhaddante tvannu dāsoti maññasi  
  
      Yassa dhenusahassāni sadā dughanti    visatiṃ  
 Okkākaputto bhaddante tvannu dāsoti maññasi  
  
      Taggha te dukkaṭaṃ bale yaṃ khattiyaṃ mahabbalaṃ  
 Nāgaṃ maṇḍukavaṇṇe na taṃ akkhāsi āgataṃ    
  
      Aparādhaṃ mahārāja tvaṃ no khama rathesabha  
 Yaṃ taṃ aññātavesena naññāsimbhā idhāgataṃ  
  
      Mādisassa na taṃ channaṃ yohaṃ aḷāriko bhave  
 Tvaññeva me pasidassu nanthi te deva dukkaṭaṃ  
  
                    
      Gaccha bale khamāpehi kusarājaṃ mahabbalaṃ  
 Khamāpito kusarājā so te dassati jīvitaṃ  
  
      Pitussa vacanaṃ sutvā devavaṇṇi pabhāvatī  
 Sirasā aggahi pāde kusarājaṃ mahabbalaṃ  
  
      Yā imā ratyo atikkantā tā imā deva tayā vinā  
 Vande te sirasā pāde mā me kujjha rathesabha  
  
      Saccaṃ te    paṭijānāmi mahārāja suṇohi me  
 Na cāpi appiyaṃ    tuyhaṃ kareyyāmi ahaṃ puna  
  
   Duhanti    machasaṃ vi syā   Nanaṃ ākkhāsimāgataṃ   machasaṃ syā 
   Sabbaṃ te   machasaṃ   Apiyaṃ   machasaṃ  
                    
      Evañce yāvamānāya vacanaṃ me na kāhasi  
 Idāni maṃ tāto havatvā khantiyānaṃ padasasti  
  
      Evante yācamānāya kiṃ na kāhāmi te vaco  
 Vikuddho tyasmi kalyāṇi mā tvaṃ bhāyi pabhāvati  
  
                    
      Saccante paṭijānāmi rājaputti suṇohi me  
 Na cāpi appiyaṃ tuyhaṃ kareyyāmi ahaṃ puna  
  
      Taca kāmā hi sussoṇi bahuṃ dukkhaṃ titikkhisaṃ  
 Pahu maddakulaṃ gantvā nayituṃ taṃ pabhāvati  
  
      Yojayantu rathe asse nānācitte samāhite  
 Atha dakkhatha me vegaṃ vidhamentassa sattavo  
  
      Tañca tattha udikkhiṃsu rañño maddassa thipure    
 Vijambhamānaṃ sīhaṃva pothentaṃ diguṇaṃ bhujaṃ  
  
                    
      Hatthakkhandhañca āruyha āropetvā pabhavatiṃ  
 Saṅgāmaṃ otaritvāna sihanādaṃ nadi kuso  
      Tassa taṃ nadato sutvā sihassevitare migā  
 Khantiyā vipalāyiṃsu kusaddasabhayaṭṭitā  
  
      Hatthārohā anikaṭṭhā rathikā pattikārakā  
 Aññamaññassa chindanti kusasaddabhayaṭṭitā  
  
      Tasmiṃ saṅghāmasisassamiṃ passitvā tuṭṭhamānaso    
 Kusassa rañño devindo adā verocanaṃ maṇi  
  
      So taṃ vijitvā saṅgāmaṃ laddhā verocanaṃ maṇiṃ  
 Hatthikkhandhagato rājā pāvekkhi nagaraṃ puraṃ  
  
      Jivagāhaṃ    gahetvāna bandhitvā satta khattiye  
 Sasurassupanāmesi ime te deva sattavo  
  
   Maddasasante pure   machasaṃ   Haṭṭhamānaso   vi machasaṃ   Jivaggāhaṃ  machasaṃ 
  
                     
      Sabbeva te vasaṅgatā amittā vihatā taca  
 Kāmaṃ karohi te tayā muñca vā te hanassu vā  
  
                    
      Tumbheva    sattavo ete nahi te myaha sattavo  
 Tvaññeva no mahārāja muñca vā te hanassu vā  
  
      Imā te dhītaro satta devakaññupamā subhā  
 Dadāhi nesaṃ ekekaṃ hontu jāmātaro taca  
  
      Ambhākañceva tvaṃ no sabbesamissaro  
 Tvaññeva no mahārāja dehi nesaṃ yadicchasi  
  
      Ekamekasasa ekekaṃ adā sihassaro kuso  
 Khattiyānaṃ tadā nesaṃ rañño maddassa dhitaro  
  
      Piṇitā    tena lābhena tuṭṭhā sihasasare kuse  
 Sakaraṭṭhāni pāyiṃsu khattiyā satta tāvade  
  
      Pabhāvatiñca ādāya maṇiṃ verocanaṃ subhaṃ  
 Kusāvatiṃ kuso rājā agamāsi mahabbalo  
  
      Tyassu ekarathe yantā pavisantā kusāvatiṃ   
 Samānā vaṇṇarūpena nāññamaññamatirocayuṃ    
  
      Mātā puttena saṅgañachi ubhayo ca jayampatī  
 Samaggā te tadā āsuṃ phītaṃ dharaṇimāvasunti  
   Kusajātakaṃ  
  
   Tuyheva   vi machasaṃ syā   Paṇitā   vi machasaṃ   Rocayiṃsu   machasaṃ 
  
                    
   Soṇanandajātakaṃ  
                    
      Devatānusi gandhabbo ādu sakko purindado  
 Manussabhuto iddhimā kathaṃ jānemu taṃ mayaṃ  
  
      Namhi devo na gandhabbo namhi sakko purindado  
 Manussabhuto iddhimā evaṃ jānāhi bhārata    
  
      Katarūpamidaṃ bhotā    veyyāvaccaṃ anappakaṃ  
 Devambhi vassamānambhi anovassaṃ bhavaṃ akā  
      Tato vātātape ḷore sitacchāyaṃ bhavaṃ akā  
 Tato amittamajjhe    ca saratāṇaṃ bhavaṃ akā  
  
      Tato phitāni raṭṭhāni vasino te bhavaṃ akā  
 Tato ekasataṃ khatye anuyante bhavaṃ akā  
  
      Patitāssu    mayaṃ bhoto vara taṃ bhaññamicchasi    
 Hatthiyānaṃ assarathaṃ nāriyo ca alaṅkatā 
 Nivesanāni rammāni mayaṃ bhoto dadāmase  
  
      Atha vā aṅge vā magadhe    mayaṃ bhoto dadāmase  
 Atha vā assakāvantiṃ sumanā damma te mayaṃ  
  
      Upaḍḍhaṃ vāpi rajjassa mayaṃ bhoto dadāmase  
 Sace te attho rajjena anusāsa yadicchasi  
  
                    
      Na me atthopi rājjena nagarena dhanena vā  
 Athopi janapadena attho mayhaṃ na vijjati  
  
      Bhotova raṭṭhe vijite araññe atthi assamo  
 Pitā mayhaṃ janetti ca ubho sammanti assame  
  
      Tesāhaṃ pubbācariyesu puññaṃ na labhāmi    kātave  
 Bhavantaṃ ajjhācaraṃ katvā soṇaṃ yācāmu    saṃvaraṃ  
  
   Bhāradha   machasaṃ   Bhoto   syā   Amittamajjhesu   machasaṃ syā 
   Patitassu   machasaṃ   Vadataṃbhuñajamicchasi   machasaṃ   Athavaṅgavā magadhe   
 machasaṃ syā   Labbhāmi   machasaṃ   Yāmecu   machasaṃ  
  
                    
      Karomi te taṃ vacanaṃ yaṃ maṃ bhaṇasi brāhmaṇa  
 Etañca kho no akkhāhi nivanto hontu yācakā  
  
                    
      Parosataṃ jānapadā    mahāsālā ca brāhmaṇā 
 Ime ca khattiyā sabbe abhijātā yasassino 
 Bhavañca rājā manojo alaṃ hessanti yācakā  
  
      Hatthi asse ca yojentu rathaṃ santayha sārathi  
 Ābandhanāni gaṇhatha pādesussārayaṃ daje 
 Assamaṃ taṃ gamissāmi yattha sammani kosiyo  
  
      Tato ca rājā pāyāsi senāya caturaṅgini  
 Agamāsi    assamaṃ rammaṃ yattha sammati kosiyo  
  
                    
      Kassa kādambayo    kājo vehāsaṃ caturaṅgulaṃ  
 Aṃsaṃ asamphusaṃ eti udabhārasasa gacchato  
  
      Ahaṃ soṇo mahārāja tāpaso sahitabbato  
 Bharāmi mātāpitaro rattindivamatandito  
  
      Vane phalañca mulañca āharitvā disampati  
 Posemi mātāpitaro pubbekatamanussaraṃ  
  
                    
      Icchāmi assamaṃ gantuṃ yattha sammati kosiyo  
 Maggaṃ no soṇa akkhāhi yena gacchemu assamaṃ  
  
      Ayaṃ ekapadi rāja yenetaṃ meghasantihaṃ  
 Akoviḷārehi sañachannaṃ ettha sammati kosiyo  
  
      Idaṃ vatvāna pakkāmi taramāno mahāisi  
 Vehāse antalikkhasmiṃ anusāsitvāna khattiye  
  
      Assamaṃ parimajjitvā paññāpetvāna āsanaṃ  
 Paṇṇasālaṃ pavisitvā pitaraṃ paṭibodhayi  
  
   Janapadā   vi machasaṃ   Agāmā   vi Machasaṃ   Kādambamayo   machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Ime āyanti rājāno abhijātā yasassino  
 Assamā nikkhamitvāna nisidāhi    mahāisi  
  
      Tassa taṃ vacanaṃ sutvā taramāno mahāisi  
 Assamā nikkhamitvāna padvārambhi upāvisi  
  
         
      Tañca disvāna āyantaṃ jalantariva tejasā  
 Khatti    saṅghaparibbuḷhaṃ kosiyo etadabravi  
      Kassa bherī mudiṅgā ca saṅkhā paṇavadeṇḍimā    
 Purato viṭapantāni hāsayantā rathesabhaṃ  
  
      Kassa kañcanapaṭṭena puthunā vijjuvaṇṇinā  
 Yuvā kalāpasannaddho ko eti siriyā jalaṃ  
  
      Ukkā mukhe    pahaṭṭhaṃva khadiraṅgārasantibhaṃ  
 Mukhañca ruciraṃ bhāti ko eti siriyā jalaṃ  
  
      Tassa pagaghitaṃ chattaṃ sasalākaṃ manoramaṃ  
 Ādiccaraṃsāvaraṇaṃ    ko eti siriyā jalaṃ  
  
      Kassa aṅgaṃ pariggayha vālavijanimuttamā  
 Caranti varapaññassa    hatthikkhandhena āyato  
  
      Kassa setāni chattāni ājāniyā ca vammitā    
 Samantā parikiranti ko eti siriyā jalaṃ  
  
      Kassa ekasataṃ khatyā anuyantā yasassino  
 Samantā anupariyanti ko eti siriyā jalaṃ  
  
      Hatthi assā rathā patti senāya caturaṅganī  
 Samantā anupariyanti ko eti siriyā jalaṃ  
  
      Kassesā mahati senā piṭṭhito anuvatattī  
 Akkhobhanī apariyantā sāgarasseva ūmiyo  
  
   Nisada tvaṃ mahā ise   vi machasaṃ syā   Khatya   machasaṃ 
   Nindimā   machasaṃ   Mukhaṃ   machasaṃ   Ādicca rasāvaraṇaṃ   machasaṃ 
   Varapuññassa   machasaṃ   Camimikā   machasaṃ 
  
                     
      Rājābhirājā manojo indeva jayataṃ pati nandassajjhāvaraṃ eti assamaṃ brahmacārinaṃ  
  
      Tassesā mahati senā piṭṭhito anuvattati  
 Akkhobhani apariyantā sāgarasseva ūmiyo  
  
                    
      Anulittā candanena kāsikuttamadhārino  
 Sabbe pañajalikā hutvā isinaṃ ajjhupāgamuṃ  
  
      Kacci nu bhoto kusalaṃ kacci bhoto anāmayaṃ  
 Kacci uñechana yāpetha kacci mulaphalā bahu  
  
      Kacci ḍaṃsā ca makasā appameva siriṃsapā  
 Vane vālamigākiṇṇe kacci hiṃsā na vijjati  
  
      Kusalañce no rāja atho rāja anāmayaṃ  
 Atho uñechana yāpema atho mulaphalā bahu  
  
      Atho ḍaṃsā ca makasā appameva siraṃsapā    
 Vane vālamigākiṇṇe hiṃsā ambhaṃ    na vijjati  
  
      Bahuni vassapugāni assame vasato    idha  
 Nābhijānāmi uppannaṃ ābādhaṃ amanoramaṃ  
  
      Svāgatante mahārāja atho te adurāgataṃ  
 Issarosi anuppatto yaṃ idhatthi pavedayaṃ    
  
                    
      Tindukāni    piyālāni madhuke kāsa    māriyo  
 Phalāni khuddakappāni bhuñja rāja varaṃ varaṃ  
  
      Idampi pāniyaṃ sītaṃ ābhataṃ girigababharā  
 Tato piva mahārāja sace tvaṃ abhikaṅkhasi  
  
      Paṭiggahitaṃ yaṃ dinnaṃ sabbassa agghiyaṃ kataṃ  
 Nandassāpi nisāmetha vacanaṃ yaṃ    pavakkhati  
  
   Sarisapā   machasaṃ   Mayhaṃ   machasaṃ   Samamato   machasaṃ sammataṃ   vi 
   Pavedhaya   machasaṃ   Tiṇḍukāni   machasaṃ   Kāsu   vi machasaṃ   So   machasaṃ  
                    
      Ajjhavarambhā nandassa bhoto santikamāgatā  
 Suṇātu me bhavaṃ vacanaṃ nandassa parisāya ca  
  
      Parosataṃ jānapadā mahāsālā ca brāhmaṇā  
 Ime ca khattiyā sabbe abhijātā yasassino 
 Bhavañca rājā manojo anumaññantu me vaco  
  
      Ye vasanti samitāro yakkhāni idha asasame  
 Araññe bhūtabhavyāni suṇantu vacanaṃ mama  
  
      Namo katvāna bhūtānaṃ isiṃ vakkhāmi subbataṃ  
 So tyāhaṃ dakkhiṇo    bāhu tava kosiya sammato  
  
      Pitaraṃ me janettiñca bhattukāmassa me sato  
 Vīra puññamidaṃ ṭhānaṃ mā maṃ kosiya vāraya  
  
                    
      Sabbhihetaṃ upaññātaṃ mametaṃ apanissaja  
 Uṭṭhānapāricariyāya dīgharattaṃ tayā kataṃ  
 Mātāpitusu puññāni mama lokadado bhava  
  
      Tatheva santi manujā dhamme dhammapadaṃ vudu    
 Maggo saggassa lokassa yathā jānāsi tvaṃ ise  
  
      Uṭṭhānapāricariyāya mātāpitu sukhāvahaṃ  
 Taṃ maṃ puññābhivāreti ariyamaggāvaro naro  
  
                    
      Suṇantu bhonto vacanaṃ bhātu    rajjhāvarā mama  
 Kulavaṃsaṃ mahārāja porāṇaṃ parihāpayaṃ 
 Adhammacāri    yo jeṭṭho nirayaṃ so upapajjati  
  
   Dakkhiṇaṃ   machasaṃ   Vida   machasaṃ   Bhāta   vi machasaṃ   Adhammacāri 
 jeṭṭhesu   machasaṃ syā adhacāri jeṭṭho   vi  
  
                    
      Ye ca dhammassa kusalā porāṇassa disampati  
 Cārintena ca sampannā na te gacchanti duggatiṃ  
  
      Mātāpitā ca bhātā ca bhagini ñātibandhavā  
 Sabbe jeṭṭhassa te bhārā evaṃ jānāhi bhārata    
  
      Ādiyitvā garuṃ bhāraṃ nāviko viya ussahe  
 Dhammañca nappamajjāmi    jeṭṭhocasmi rathesabha  
  
      Adhigatambhā    tame ñāṇaṃ jālaṃva jātavedato    
 Evameva no bhavaṃ dhammaṃ kosiyo pavidaṃsayi  
  
      Yathā udayamādicco vāsudevo pabhaṅkaro  
 Pāṇinaṃ pavidaṃseti rūpaṃ kalyāṇapāpakaṃ 
 Evameva no bhavaṃ dhammaṃ kosiyo pavidaṃsayi  
  
                    
      Evaṃ me yācamānassa añjaliṃ nāvakhujjhatha  
 Tava baddhacaro    hessaṃ vuṭṭhito paricārako    
  
      Addhā nanda pajānāsi saddhammaṃ sabbhi desitaṃ  
 Ariyo ariyasamācāro bāḷhaṃ tvaṃ mama ruccasi  
      Bhavantaṃ vadāmi bhotiñca suṇātha vacanaṃ mama  
 Nāyaṃ bhāro bhāramatto ahu mayhaṃ kudācanaṃ  
  
   Bhāradha   machasaṃ   Pamajjāmina   machasaṃ   Adhigamā   machasaṃ adhigamahā 
   syā   Jātavedaso   machasaṃ   Tavupaṭṭhacaro   machasaṃ tavapaṭṭhavaro  syā   
 Paricāriko   machasaṃ  
  
                    
      Taṃ maṃ upaṭṭhitaṃ santaṃ mātāpitu sukhāvahaṃ  
 Nando ajjhācaraṃ katvā upaṭṭhānāya yācati  
  
                    
      Yo ce icchati kāmena santānaṃ brahmacārinaṃ  
 Nandaṃ vo caratha eko kaṃ nando upatiṭṭhatu  
  
      Tayā tāta anuññātā soṇa taṃ nissitā mayaṃ  
 Upaghāyituṃ    labhe nandaṃ muddhani brahmacārinaṃ  
  
      Assatthasseva taruṇaṃ pavāḷaṃ māḷuteritaṃ  
 Cirassa nandaṃ disvāna hadayaṃ me pavedhati  
  
      Yadā suttāpi supine    nandaṃ passāmi āgataṃ  
 Udaggā sumanā homi nando no āgato ayaṃ  
  
      Yadā ca paṭikhujjhitvā nandaṃ passāmi nāgataṃ  
 Bhiyo    āvisati soko domanassañcanappakaṃ  
  
                    
      Sāhaṃ ajja cirassampi nandaṃ passāmi āgataṃ  
 Bhattu ca mayhañca piyo nando no pāvisi gharaṃ  
  
      Pitu ca    nando suppiyo    yaṃ nando nappavase gharā    
 Labhatu tāta nando taṃ maṃ nando upatiṭṭhatu  
  
      Anukampikā patiṭṭhā ca pubbe rasadadi ca no  
 Maggo saggassa lokassa mātā taṃ varate ise  
  
      Pubbe rasadadi gonti mātā puññupasañahitā  
 Maggo saggassa lokassa mātā taṃ varate ise  
  
                    
      Ākakkhamānā puttaphalaṃ devatāya namassati nakkhantāni ca pucchati 
 utusaṃvaccharāni ca  
  
      Tassā atusinātāya hoti gabbhassavakkamo    
 Tena dohaḷini hoti suhadā tena vuccati  
  
   Upaghātuṃ   machasaṃ syā   Suppanne   machasaṃ syā 
   Hiyo   machasaṃ   Pitupi   vi machasaṃ   Supiyo   machasaṃ 
   Gharaṃ   machasaṃ syā   Anukamapakā   machasaṃ syā  
   Vokkamo   vi machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Saṃvaccharaṃ vā ūnaṃ vā pariharitvā vijāyati  
 Tena sā janayantiti janetti tena vuccati  
  
      Thanakkhirena gitena aṅgapāpūraṇena ca  
 Rodantaṃ puttaṃ toseti    tosenti tena vuccati  
  
      Tato vātātape ghore mamaṃ    katvā udikkhati  
 Dārakaṃ appajānantaṃ    posenti tena vuccati  
  
      Yañca mātu dhanaṃ hoti yaññaca hoti pituddhanaṃ  
 Ubhayampetassa gopeti api puttassa no siyā 
 Evaṃ puttaṃ aduṃ putta iti mātā vihaññati  
  
      Pamattaṃ paradāresu nisithe    pattayobbane  
 Sāyaṃ puttaṃ anāyantaṃ iti matā vihaññati  
  
      Evaṃ kicchā bhato poso mātu aparivārako  
 Mātarī micchā caritvāna nirayaṃ so upapajjati  
  
      Evaṃ kicchā bhato poso pitu aparivārako  
 Mātaraṃ aparicaritvāna kicchaṃ vā so upapajjati  
  
      Dhanāpi    dhanakāmānaṃ nassati iti me sutaṃ  
 Mātaraṃ aparicaritvāna kicchaṃ vā so nigacchati  
  
      Dhanāpi dhanakāmānaṃ nassati iti me sutaṃ  
 Pitaraṃ aparicaritvāna kicchaṃ vā so nigacchati  
  
      Ānando ca pamādo ca sadā hasitakīḷitaṃ  
 Mātaraṃ paricaritvāna labbhametaṃ    vijānato  
  
   Tosenti   vi machasaṃ   Mammaṃ   machasaṃ mamiṃ   vi   Apajānattaṃ   vi machasaṃ 
   Niside   machasaṃ nissive   syā   Aparicāriko   machasaṃ 
   Dhanaṃpi   machasaṃ syā   Labbatena   machasaṃ syā 
  
                        Ānando ca pamādo ca sadā hasitakīḷitaṃ  
 Pītaraṃ paricaritvāna labbhametaṃ vijānato  
  
      Dānañca piyavācā ca atthacariyā ca yā idha  
 Samānattatā ca dhammesu tattha tattha yathārahaṃ  
  
      Ete kho saṃgahā loke rathassāṇiva yāyato  
 Ete ca saṅghahā nāssu na mātā puttakāraṇā 
 Uabhetha mānaṃ pūjaṃ vā pitā vā puttakāraṇā  
                    
  
      Yasmā ca saṅgahā    ete samavekkhanti paṇḍitā  
 Tsamā mahantaṃ papponti pāsaṃsā    ca bhavanti te  
  
      Brahmamāti mātāpitaro pubbācariyāti vuccare  
 Āhunaiyyā ca puttānaṃ pajāya anukampakā  
  
      Tasmā hi te namasseyya sakkareyyātha    paṇḍito  
 Annena atho pānena vatthena sayanena ca 
 Ucchādanena nahāpanne pādānaṃ dhovanena ca  
  
      Tāya naṃ pāricariyāya mātāpitusu paṇḍitā    
 Idheva    pasaṃsanti pecca sagge pamodatiti  
   Soṇanandajātakaṃ  
  
 Sattatinipāto niṭṭhito  
 Tassuddānaṃ  
 Atha sattatimmahi nipātavare 
 Sa bhavaṃ tu kusāvati rājavaro  
 Atha soṇanandavaro ca puna 
 Abhivāsita sattatimambhi suteti  
  
   Saṅghahe   machasaṃ   Pasaṃsā   vi machasaṃ   Sakakareyyava   machasaṃ 
   Paṇḍito   machasaṃ   Idhaceva   vi  
  
                    
 Asītinipāto 
   Cullahaṃsajātakaṃ  
                    
      Sumukha anupacinantā pakkamanti vibhaṅgamā  
 Gaccha tuvampi mā kaṅkhi natthi baddhe    sahāyatā  
  
      Gacchevāhaṃ na vā gacche na tena amaro siyaṃ  
 Sukhitaṃ taṃ upāsitvā sukkhitaṃ taṃ kathaṃ rahe  
  
      Maraṇaṃ vā tayā saddhiṃ jīvitaṃ vā tayā vinā  
 Tadeva maraṇaṃ seyyo yañce jive tayā vinā    
  
      Nesa dhammo mahārāja yaṃ taṃ evaṃ gataṃ    jahe  
 Yā gati tuyhaṃ sā mayhaṃ ruccate vihagādhipa    
  
      Kā nu pāsena baddhassa    gati aññā mahānasā  
 Sā kathaṃ cetayānassa muttassa tava ruccati  
  
      Kaṃ vā tvaṃ passase atthaṃ mama tuyhañca pakkhima  
 Ñātinaṃ vāvasiṭṭhānaṃ ubhintaṃ jīvitakkhaye  
  
      Yaṃ nu kañcanadepiccha    andhena tamasā gataṃ  
 Tādise sañcajaṃ pāṇaṃ kamatthamahijotaye  
  
      Kathannu patataṃ seṭṭha dhamme atthaṃ na khujjhase  
 Dhammo apavito santo atthaṃ dasseti pāṇinaṃ  
  
                 ra  
      Sohaṃ dhammaṃ avekkhanto dhammā catthaṃ samuṭṭhitaṃ  
 Bhattiñca tayi sampassaṃ nāvakaṅkhāmi jivataṃ  
  
      Addhā eso sataṃ dhammo yo mitetā mittamāpade  
 Naccaje jīvitasasāpi hetu dhammaṃ anussaraṃ  
      Svāyaṃ dhamemā ca te ciṇṇo hatti ca viditā mayi  
 Kāmaṃ karassu mayhetaṃ gacchevānumato mayā  
   Natthi bandhe   machasaṃ   Kataṃ   machasaṃ   Vihaṅgādhipa   machasaṃ   Bandhassa 
   machasaṃ   Cepiñcha   machasaṃ   Ayaṃ gāthā pādo maramma potthakesu na disasti  
                    
      Api tvevaṃ gate kāle yaṃ baddhaṃ ñātinaṃ mayā  
 Tayā taṃ buddhisampanna assa paramaṃvutaṃ  
  
      Iccevaṃ mantayantānaṃ ariyānaṃ ariyavuttinaṃ  
 Paccadissatha nesādo āturānamivantako  
  
      Te sattuṃ abhisaṃcikkha digharattaṃ hitā dijā  
 Tuṇhimāsittha ubhayo na ca sañcesumāsanā  
  
      Dhataraṭṭhe ca disvāna samuḍḍhente tato tato  
 Abhikkamatha vegena dvijasattu dvijādhipe  
  
      So ca vegenabhikkamma āsajja parame dije  
 Paccakampittha nesādo baddhā iti vicintayaṃ  
  
      Ekañca baddhimāsinaṃ abaddhañca punāparaṃ  
 Āsajja baddhamāsinaṃ pekkhamānamadinavaṃ  
  
      Tato so vimato yeva paṇḍare ajjhabhāsatha  
 Pavaddhakāye āsine dijasaṅghagaṇādhipe  
  
      Yannu pāsena mahatā baddho na kurute disaṃ  
 Atha kasmā abaddho tvaṃ bali pakkhī na gacchasi  
  
      Kinnu tāyaṃ dijo hoti mutto baddhaṃ upāsasi  
 Ohāya sakuṇā yanti kiṃ eko avahiyasi  
  
      Rājā meso dijāmitta sakhā pāṇasamo ca me  
 Neva naṃ vijahissāmi yāva kālassa pariyāyaṃ  
  
                    
      Kathaṃ panāyaṃ vihago nāddasā pāsamoḍḍitaṃ  
 Padaṃ hetaṃ mahantānaṃ boddhumarahanti āpadaṃ  
  
      Yadā parābhavo hoti poso jīvitasaṅkaye  
 Atha jālañca pāsañca āsājjapi na khujjhati  
  
      Api tveva mahāpañña pāsā bahuvidhā tatā  
 Gulhamāsajja bajjhanti athevaṃ jīvitakkhaye  
  
                    
                    
      Apināyaṃ tayā saddhiṃ sambhāsassa sukhudrayo  
 Api no anumaññasi api no jīvitaṃ dade  
  
      Na ceva me tvaṃ baddhosi napi icchāmi te vadhaṃ  
 Kāmaṃ khippamito gantvā jiva tvaṃ anigho ciraṃ  
  
      Na vāhametaṃ    icchāmi aññatretassa jīvitā  
 Sace ekena tuṭṭhosi muñcetaṃ mañca bhakkhaya  
      Ārohapariṇāhena tulyasmā vayasā ubho  
 Na te lābhena jinatthi    etena niminā tuvaṃ  
  
      Tadiṅgha samavekkhassu hotu giddhi tavāsmasu  
 Maṃ pubbe bandha pāsena pacchā muñca dijādhipaṃ  
      Tāvadeva ca te lābho katassa yācanāya ca  
 Mitti ca dhataraṭṭhehi yāvajivāya te siyā  
  
      Passantu no mahāsaṅghā tayā muttaṃ ito gataṃ  
 Mittāmaccā ca bhattā ca puttadārā ca bandhavā  
  
      Na ca te tādisā mittā bahuntaṃ    idha vijjati  
 Yathā tvaṃ dhataraṭṭhassa pāṇasādhāraṇo sakhā  
  
      So te sahāyaṃ muñcāmi hotu rājā tavānugo  
 Kāmaṃ khippamito gantvā ñātimajjhe virocatha  
  
      So patito pamuttena bhattunā bhattu gāravo  
 Ajjhabhāsatha vakkaṅgo vācaṃ kaṇṇasukhaṃ bhaṇaṃ  
  
      Evaṃ luddaka nandassa saha sabbehi ñātihi  
 Yathāhamajja nandāmi muttaṃ disvā dijādhipaṃ  
  
      Ehi taṃ anusikkhāmi yathā tuvampi lacchase  
 Lābhaṃ yathāyaṃ    dhataraṭṭho pāpaṃ kiñci na dakkhati  
  
      Khippamante puraṃ netvā    rañño dassehi no ubho  
 Abaddhe pakatībhute kāje ubhayate ṭhite 
  
   Nevāhaṃ   machasaṃ   Jivatthi   machasaṃ   Bahunaṃ   machasaṃ   Tavāya  machasaṃ 
 syā   Gantvā   machasaṃ syā  
  
                    
      Dhataraṭṭhā mahārāja haṃsādhipatino ime  
 Ayaṃ hi rājā haṃsānaṃ ayaṃ senāpatitaro  
  
      Asaṃsayaṃ imaṃ disvā haṃsarājaṃ narādhipo  
 Patitā sumano vitto bahuṃ dassati te dhanaṃ  
  
                    
      Tassa taṃ vacanaṃ sutvā kammanā    upapādayi  
 Khippamantepuraṃ gantvā rañño haṃse adassiyi  
 Abaddhe pakatibhute kāje ubhayato ṭhite  
  
      Dhataraṭṭhā mahārāja haṃsādhipatino ime  
 Ayaṃ hi rājā haṃsānaṃ ayaṃ senāpatitaro  
  
      Kathaṃ panidhe vihagā    tava hatthatthamāgatā  
 Kathaṃ luddo mahantānaṃ issaremidhamajjhagā  
  
      Vihitā santi me pāsā pallalesu janādhipa  
 Yaṃ yadāyatanaṃ maññe dijānaṃ pāṇarodhanaṃ  
  
      Tādisaṃ pāsamāsajja haṃsarājā abajjhatha  
 Taṃ abaddho upāsino mamāyaṃ ajjhabhāsatha  
  
      Sudukkaraṃ anariyehi dahate bhāvamuttamaṃ  
 Bhatturatthe parakkanto dhamme yutto vihaṅgamo  
  
      Attanāyaṃ cajitvāna jīvitaṃ jīvitāraho  
 Anutthunanto āsino bhattu yācittha jīvitaṃ  
  
      Tassa taṃ vacanaṃ sutvā pasādamahamajjhagaṃ  
 Tato naṃ pāmuviṃ pāsā anuññāsiṃ sukhena ca  
  
      So patito pamuttena battunā bhattugāraco  
 Ajjhaśasatha vakkaṅgo vācaṃ kaṇṇasukhaṃ bhaṇaṃ  
  
   Kammamunā   machasaṃ syā   Vibhaṅga   machasaṃ syā 
  
                    
      Evaṃ luddaka nandassu saha sabbehi ñātibhi  
 Yathāhamajja nandami muttaṃ disvā dijādhipaṃ  
  
      Ehi taṃ anusikkhāmi yathā tvamapi lacchase  
 Lābhaṃ yathāyaṃ dhataraṭṭho pāpaṃ kiñci nadakkhati    
  
      Khippamantepuraṃ gantvā rañño dassehi no ubho  
 Abaddhe pakatibhūte kāje uīyato ṭhite  
  
      Dhataraṭṭhā mahārāja haṃsādhipatino ime  
 Ayaṃ hi rājā haṃsānaṃ ayaṃ senāpatitaro  
  
      Asaṃsayaṃ imaṃ disvā haṃsarājaṃ narādhipo  
 Patito sumano vitto bahuṃ dasasti te dhanaṃ  
  
                    
      Evametassa vacanā ānitāme ubho mayā  
 Ettheva hi ime assu ubho anumatā mayā  
  
      Soyaṃ evaṃ gato pakkhī dijo paramadhammiko  
 Mādisassa hi luddassa janayeyyātha maddavaṃ  
  
      Upāyanaṃ hi    te deva nāññaṃ passāmi edisaṃ  
 Sabbasākuṇikagāme taṃ passa manujādhipa  
  
                    
      Disvā nisinnaṃ rājānaṃ piṭhe sovaṇṇaye subhe  
 Ajjhabhāsatha vakkaṅgo vācaṃ kaṇṇasukhaṃ bhaṇaṃ  
  
      Kaccinu bhoto kusalaṃ kacci bhoto anāmayaṃ  
 Kacci raṭṭhamidaṃ phītaṃ dhammena manusisasati    
  
      Kusalañceva me haṃsa atho haṃsa anāmayaṃ  
 Atho raṭṭhamidaṃ phītaṃ dhammena manusisasti  
  
      Kacci bhoto amaccesu doso koci na vijjati  
 Kaccinnu te tavatthesu nāvakaṅkhanti jīvitaṃ 
  
      Athopi me amaccesu doso koci na vijjati  
 Atho te mamatthesu nāvakaṅkhanti jīvitaṃ  
  
   Nadakkhasi   machasaṃ   Ca   machasaṃ   Manusāsati   machasaṃ syā 
                     
      Kacci te sādisi bhariyā assavā piyabhāṇini  
 Puttarūpayasupetā tava chandamasānugā  
  
      Atho me sādisi bhariyā assavā piyyāṇinī  
 Puttarūpayasupetā mama chandavasānugā  
  
                    
      Bhavaṃ tu kacci nu mahāsattuhatthatthataṅgato
